 // Handle edit and delete actions
 function handleConnectionAction(e) {
+  // Handle anchor click for create-connection
+  const anchor = e.target.closest('a[data-action]');
+  if (anchor) {
+    e.preventDefault();
+    const action = anchor.dataset.action;
+    if (action === 'create-connection') {
+      // Get the platform type from the data attribute
+      const platformType = anchor.dataset.platformType || null;
+      // Open the Edit Connections modal to allow creating/enabling the connection
+      if (typeof openEditConnectionsModal === 'function') {
+        openEditConnectionsModal(platformType);
+      }
+    }
+    return;
+  }
+  
   const btn = e.target.closest('button[data-action]');

+// ==================== EDIT CONNECTIONS MODAL ====================
+
+// Open Edit Connections Modal
+// platformTypeFilter: 'DSP', 'Ad Server', or null (show all)
+function openEditConnectionsModal(platformTypeFilter) {
+  const modal = document.getElementById('editConnectionsModal');
+  if (!modal) return;
+
+  // Reset all checkboxes and toggles first
+  resetEditConnectionsModal();
+
+  // Show/hide sections based on platform type filter
+  const dspSection = document.getElementById('editDspSection');
+  const adServerSection = document.getElementById('editAdServerSection');
+  
+  // Get all DSP connector cards
+  const dspCards = modal.querySelectorAll('.connector-card[data-connector="trade-desk"], .connector-card[data-connector="dv360"], .connector-card[data-connector="simplifi"]');
+  // Get all Ad Server connector cards
+  const adServerCards = modal.querySelectorAll('.connector-card[data-connector="google-campaign-manager"]');
+  
+  if (platformTypeFilter === 'DSP') {
+    // Show only DSP section
+    if (dspSection) dspSection.style.display = '';
+    dspCards.forEach(card => card.style.display = '');
+    if (adServerSection) adServerSection.style.display = 'none';
+    adServerCards.forEach(card => card.style.display = 'none');
+  } else if (platformTypeFilter === 'Ad Server') {
+    // Show only Ad Server section
+    if (dspSection) dspSection.style.display = 'none';
+    dspCards.forEach(card => card.style.display = 'none');
+    if (adServerSection) adServerSection.style.display = '';
+    adServerCards.forEach(card => card.style.display = '');
+  } else {
+    // Show all sections (no filter)
+    if (dspSection) dspSection.style.display = '';
+    dspCards.forEach(card => card.style.display = '');
+    if (adServerSection) adServerSection.style.display = '';
+    adServerCards.forEach(card => card.style.display = '');
+  }
+
+  // Read current connections from the table
+  const tableBody = document.getElementById('campaignTableBody');
+  if (tableBody) {
+    const rows = tableBody.querySelectorAll('tr[data-platform]');
+    
+    // Map platform display names to checkbox values
+    const platformValueMap = {
+      'Trade Desk': 'trade-desk',
+      'The Trade Desk': 'trade-desk',
+      'DV360': 'dv360',
+      'Display & Video 360': 'dv360',
+      'Simplifi': 'simplifi',
+      'Google Campaign Manager': 'google-campaign-manager'
+    };
+    
+    rows.forEach(row => {
+      const platformName = row.getAttribute('data-platform');
+      const platformValue = platformValueMap[platformName] || platformName;
+      
+      // Find the corresponding checkbox in the modal
+      const checkbox = modal.querySelector(`input[value="${platformValue}"]`);
+      if (checkbox) {
+        checkbox.checked = true;
+        
+        // Update the card styling
+        const card = checkbox.closest('.connector-card');
+        if (card) {
+          card.classList.add('selected', 'border-blue-500', 'bg-blue-50');
+        }
+        
+        // Find if this row is connected (synced)
+        // Look for "Create" link - if present, it's disconnected
+        const createLink = row.querySelector('a[data-action="create-connection"]');
+        const isConnected = !createLink;
+        
+        // Find the toggle button for this connector
+        const toggle = modal.querySelector(`.edit-connector-toggle[data-connector="${platformValue}"]`);
+        if (toggle) {
+          updateToggleState(toggle, isConnected);
+        }
+      }
+    });
+  }
+
+  // Show the modal
+  modal.classList.remove('hidden');
+  modal.classList.add('flex');
+}
+
+// Reset the Edit Connections Modal to default state
+function resetEditConnectionsModal() {
+  const modal = document.getElementById('editConnectionsModal');
+  if (!modal) return;
+
+  // Reset all checkboxes
+  modal.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]').forEach(cb => {
+    cb.checked = false;
+  });
+
+  // Reset all connector cards
+  modal.querySelectorAll('.connector-card').forEach(card => {
+    card.classList.remove('selected', 'border-blue-500', 'bg-blue-50');
+  });
+
+  // Reset all toggles
+  modal.querySelectorAll('.edit-connector-toggle').forEach(toggle => {
+    updateToggleState(toggle, false);
+  });
+
+  // Reset master toggle
+  const masterToggle = document.getElementById('editConnectorsToggle');
+  if (masterToggle) {
+    updateToggleState(masterToggle, false);
+  }
+}
+
+// Update toggle button state
+function updateToggleState(toggle, isEnabled) {
+  const span = toggle.querySelector('span[aria-hidden="true"]');
+  const statusLabel = toggle.closest('.connector-card')?.querySelector('.connector-status-label');
+  
+  if (isEnabled) {
+    toggle.classList.remove('bg-gray-200');
+    toggle.classList.add('bg-blue-600');
+    toggle.setAttribute('aria-checked', 'true');
+    if (span) {
+      span.classList.remove('translate-x-0');
+      span.classList.add('translate-x-5');
+    }
+    if (statusLabel) {
+      statusLabel.textContent = 'Synced';
+      statusLabel.classList.remove('text-gray-600');
+      statusLabel.classList.add('text-green-600');
+    }
+  } else {
+    toggle.classList.remove('bg-blue-600');
+    toggle.classList.add('bg-gray-200');
+    toggle.setAttribute('aria-checked', 'false');
+    if (span) {
+      span.classList.remove('translate-x-5');
+      span.classList.add('translate-x-0');
+    }
+    if (statusLabel) {
+      statusLabel.textContent = 'Not Synced';
+      statusLabel.classList.remove('text-green-600');
+      statusLabel.classList.add('text-gray-600');
+    }
+  }
+}
+
+// Close Edit Connections Modal
+function closeEditConnectionsModal() {
+  const modal = document.getElementById('editConnectionsModal');
+  if (modal) {
+    modal.classList.add('hidden');
+    modal.classList.remove('flex');
+  }
+}
+
+// Save Edit Connections
+function saveEditConnections() {
+  const modal = document.getElementById('editConnectionsModal');
+  if (!modal) return;
+
+  // Get current ad group
+  const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
+  const adGroupId = urlParams.get('adGroupId');
+  
+  if (!adGroupId) {
+    if (window.toast && typeof window.toast.error === 'function') {
+      window.toast.error('Ad Group ID not found');
+    }
+    return;
+  }
+
+  try {
+    const data = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('adgroups_data_v1') || '[]');
+    let adGroup = data.find(ag => ag.id === adGroupId);
+
+    if (!adGroup) {
+      if (window.toast && typeof window.toast.error === 'function') {
+        window.toast.error('Ad Group not found');
+      }
+      return;
+    }
+
+    // Collect selected platforms and their status from the modal
+    const selectedDSP = [];
+    const selectedAdServer = [];
+    const connectionStatus = {};
+
+    modal.querySelectorAll('.connector-card').forEach(card => {
+      const checkbox = card.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"]');
+      const toggle = card.querySelector('.edit-connector-toggle');
+      
+      if (checkbox && checkbox.checked) {
+        const connectorType = checkbox.name; // 'edit-dsp' or 'edit-adserver'
+        const connectorValue = checkbox.value;
+        const isConnected = toggle && toggle.getAttribute('aria-checked') === 'true';
+        
+        if (connectorType === 'edit-dsp') {
+          selectedDSP.push(connectorValue);
+        } else if (connectorType === 'edit-adserver') {
+          selectedAdServer.push(connectorValue);
+        }
+        
+        connectionStatus[connectorValue] = isConnected ? 'Connected' : 'Disconnected';
+      }
+    });
+
+    // Update ad group connectors
+    adGroup.connectors = {
+      dsp: selectedDSP,
+      adServer: selectedAdServer,
+      status: connectionStatus
+    };
+
+    // Save back to localStorage
+    localStorage.setItem('adgroups_data_v1', JSON.stringify(data));
+
+    // Show success message
+    if (window.toast && typeof window.toast.success === 'function') {
+      window.toast.success('Connections updated successfully');
+    }
+
+    // Close the modal
+    closeEditConnectionsModal();
+
+    // Reload the connections table
+    loadAdGroupConnections(adGroup);
+
+  } catch (error) {
+    console.error('Error saving connections:', error);
+    if (window.toast && typeof window.toast.error === 'function') {
+      window.toast.error('Failed to save connections');
+    }
+  }
+}
+
+// Initialize Edit Connections Modal event listeners
+function initEditConnectionsModal() {
+  const modal = document.getElementById('editConnectionsModal');
+  if (!modal) return;
+
+  // Close button
+  const closeBtn = document.getElementById('closeEditConnectionsModal');
+  if (closeBtn) {
+    closeBtn.addEventListener('click', closeEditConnectionsModal);
+  }
+
+  // Cancel button
+  const cancelBtn = document.getElementById('cancelEditConnections');
+  if (cancelBtn) {
+    cancelBtn.addEventListener('click', closeEditConnectionsModal);
+  }
+
+  // Save button
+  const saveBtn = document.getElementById('saveEditConnections');
+  if (saveBtn) {
+    saveBtn.addEventListener('click', saveEditConnections);
+  }
+
+  // Close on backdrop click
+  modal.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
+    if (e.target === modal) {
+      closeEditConnectionsModal();
+    }
+  });
+
+  // Connector card click handling (toggle checkbox)
+  modal.querySelectorAll('.connector-card').forEach(card => {
+    card.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
+      // Don't toggle if clicking on the checkbox, toggle button, or their children
+      if (e.target.closest('input[type="checkbox"]') || e.target.closest('.edit-connector-toggle')) {
+        return;
+      }
+      
+      const checkbox = card.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"]');
+      if (checkbox) {
+        checkbox.checked = !checkbox.checked;
+        
+        // Update card styling
+        if (checkbox.checked) {
+          card.classList.add('selected', 'border-blue-500', 'bg-blue-50');
+        } else {
+          card.classList.remove('selected', 'border-blue-500', 'bg-blue-50');
+        }
+      }
+    });
+  });
+
+  // Checkbox change handler
+  modal.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]').forEach(checkbox => {
+    checkbox.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
+      const card = checkbox.closest('.connector-card');
+      if (card) {
+        if (checkbox.checked) {
+          card.classList.add('selected', 'border-blue-500', 'bg-blue-50');
+        } else {
+          card.classList.remove('selected', 'border-blue-500', 'bg-blue-50');
+        }
+      }
+    });
+  });
+
+  // Individual connector toggle handling
+  modal.querySelectorAll('.edit-connector-toggle').forEach(toggle => {
+    toggle.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
+      e.stopPropagation();
+      const isCurrentlyEnabled = toggle.getAttribute('aria-checked') === 'true';
+      updateToggleState(toggle, !isCurrentlyEnabled);
+    });
+  });
+
+  // Master toggle handling
+  const masterToggle = document.getElementById('editConnectorsToggle');
+  if (masterToggle) {
+    masterToggle.addEventListener('click', () => {
+      const isCurrentlyEnabled = masterToggle.getAttribute('aria-checked') === 'true';
+      const newState = !isCurrentlyEnabled;
+      
+      // Update master toggle
+      updateToggleState(masterToggle, newState);
+      
+      // Update all checked connector toggles
+      modal.querySelectorAll('.connector-card').forEach(card => {
+        const checkbox = card.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"]');
+        const toggle = card.querySelector('.edit-connector-toggle');
+        
+        if (checkbox && checkbox.checked && toggle) {
+          updateToggleState(toggle, newState);
+        }
+      });
+    });
+  }
+}
+
+// Initialize Edit Connections modal when DOM is ready
+document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', initEditConnectionsModal);
+
+// ==================== NEW CONNECTION MODAL ====================
+
+// Open New Connection Modal
+function openNewConnectionModal() {
+  const modal = document.getElementById('newConnectionModal');
+  if (!modal) return;
+
+  // Reset all checkboxes and toggles first
+  resetNewConnectionModal();
+
+  // Show the modal
+  modal.classList.remove('hidden');
+  modal.classList.add('flex');
+}
+
+// Reset the New Connection Modal to default state
+function resetNewConnectionModal() {
+  const modal = document.getElementById('newConnectionModal');
+  if (!modal) return;
+
+  // Reset all checkboxes
+  modal.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]').forEach(cb => {
+    cb.checked = false;
+  });
+
+  // Reset all connector cards
+  modal.querySelectorAll('.connector-card').forEach(card => {
+    card.classList.remove('selected', 'border-blue-500', 'bg-blue-50');
+  });
+
+  // Reset all toggles
+  modal.querySelectorAll('.new-connector-toggle').forEach(toggle => {
+    updateToggleState(toggle, false);
+  });
+
+  // Reset master toggle
+  const masterToggle = document.getElementById('newConnectorsToggle');
+  if (masterToggle) {
+    updateToggleState(masterToggle, false);
+  }
+}
+
+// Close New Connection Modal
+function closeNewConnectionModal() {
+  const modal = document.getElementById('newConnectionModal');
+  if (modal) {
+    modal.classList.add('hidden');
+    modal.classList.remove('flex');
+  }
+}
+
+// Connect (Save) New Connections
+function connectNewConnections() {
+  const modal = document.getElementById('newConnectionModal');
+  if (!modal) return;
+
+  // Get current ad group
+  const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
+  const adGroupId = urlParams.get('adGroupId');
+  
+  if (!adGroupId) {
+    if (window.toast && typeof window.toast.error === 'function') {
+      window.toast.error('Ad Group ID not found');
+    }
+    return;
+  }
+
+  try {
+    const data = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('adgroups_data_v1') || '[]');
+    let adGroup = data.find(ag => ag.id === adGroupId);
+
+    if (!adGroup) {
+      if (window.toast && typeof window.toast.error === 'function') {
+        window.toast.error('Ad Group not found');
+      }
+      return;
+    }
+
+    // Initialize connectors if not exists
+    if (!adGroup.connectors) {
+      adGroup.connectors = { dsp: [], adServer: [], status: {} };
+    }
+    if (!adGroup.connectors.dsp) adGroup.connectors.dsp = [];
+    if (!adGroup.connectors.adServer) adGroup.connectors.adServer = [];
+    if (!adGroup.connectors.status) adGroup.connectors.status = {};
+
+    // Collect selected platforms and their status from the modal
+    let newConnectionsAdded = 0;
+
+    modal.querySelectorAll('.connector-card').forEach(card => {
+      const checkbox = card.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"]');
+      const toggle = card.querySelector('.new-connector-toggle');
+      
+      if (checkbox && checkbox.checked) {
+        const connectorType = checkbox.name; // 'new-dsp' or 'new-adserver'
+        const connectorValue = checkbox.value;
+        const isConnected = toggle && toggle.getAttribute('aria-checked') === 'true';
+        
+        // Add to appropriate array if not already present
+        if (connectorType === 'new-dsp') {
+          if (!adGroup.connectors.dsp.includes(connectorValue)) {
+            adGroup.connectors.dsp.push(connectorValue);
+            newConnectionsAdded++;
+          }
+        } else if (connectorType === 'new-adserver') {
+          if (!adGroup.connectors.adServer.includes(connectorValue)) {
+            adGroup.connectors.adServer.push(connectorValue);
+            newConnectionsAdded++;
+          }
+        }
+        
+        // Update connection status
+        adGroup.connectors.status[connectorValue] = isConnected ? 'Connected' : 'Disconnected';
+      }
+    });
+
+    if (newConnectionsAdded === 0) {
+      if (window.toast && typeof window.toast.info === 'function') {
+        window.toast.info('No new connections selected');
+      }
+      return;
+    }
+
+    // Save back to localStorage
+    localStorage.setItem('adgroups_data_v1', JSON.stringify(data));
+
+    // Show success message
+    if (window.toast && typeof window.toast.success === 'function') {
+      window.toast.success(`${newConnectionsAdded} connection(s) added successfully`);
+    }
+
+    // Close the modal
+    closeNewConnectionModal();
+
+    // Reload the connections table
+    loadAdGroupConnections(adGroup);
+
+  } catch (error) {
+    console.error('Error adding connections:', error);
+    if (window.toast && typeof window.toast.error === 'function') {
+      window.toast.error('Failed to add connections');
+    }
+  }
+}
+
+// Initialize New Connection Modal event listeners
+function initNewConnectionModal() {
+  const modal = document.getElementById('newConnectionModal');
+  if (!modal) return;
+
+  // Close button
+  const closeBtn = document.getElementById('closeNewConnectionModal');
+  if (closeBtn) {
+    closeBtn.addEventListener('click', closeNewConnectionModal);
+  }
+
+  // Cancel button
+  const cancelBtn = document.getElementById('cancelNewConnection');
+  if (cancelBtn) {
+    cancelBtn.addEventListener('click', closeNewConnectionModal);
+  }
+
+  // Connect button
+  const connectBtn = document.getElementById('connectNewConnection');
+  if (connectBtn) {
+    connectBtn.addEventListener('click', connectNewConnections);
+  }
+
+  // Close on backdrop click
+  modal.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
+    if (e.target === modal) {
+      closeNewConnectionModal();
+    }
+  });
+
+  // Connector card click handling (toggle checkbox)
+  modal.querySelectorAll('.connector-card').forEach(card => {
+    card.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
+      // Don't toggle if clicking on the checkbox, toggle button, or their children
+      if (e.target.closest('input[type="checkbox"]') || e.target.closest('.new-connector-toggle')) {
+        return;
+      }
+      
+      const checkbox = card.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"]');
+      if (checkbox) {
+        checkbox.checked = !checkbox.checked;
+        
+        // Update card styling
+        if (checkbox.checked) {
+          card.classList.add('selected', 'border-blue-500', 'bg-blue-50');
+        } else {
+          card.classList.remove('selected', 'border-blue-500', 'bg-blue-50');
+        }
+      }
+    });
+  });
+
+  // Checkbox change handler
+  modal.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]').forEach(checkbox => {
+    checkbox.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
+      const card = checkbox.closest('.connector-card');
+      if (card) {
+        if (checkbox.checked) {
+          card.classList.add('selected', 'border-blue-500', 'bg-blue-50');
+        } else {
+          card.classList.remove('selected', 'border-blue-500', 'bg-blue-50');
+        }
+      }
+    });
+  });
+
+  // Individual connector toggle handling
+  modal.querySelectorAll('.new-connector-toggle').forEach(toggle => {
+    toggle.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
+      e.stopPropagation();
+      const isCurrentlyEnabled = toggle.getAttribute('aria-checked') === 'true';
+      updateToggleState(toggle, !isCurrentlyEnabled);
+    });
+  });
+
+  // Master toggle handling
+  const masterToggle = document.getElementById('newConnectorsToggle');
+  if (masterToggle) {
+    masterToggle.addEventListener('click', () => {
+      const isCurrentlyEnabled = masterToggle.getAttribute('aria-checked') === 'true';
+      const newState = !isCurrentlyEnabled;
+      
+      // Update master toggle
+      updateToggleState(masterToggle, newState);
+      
+      // Update all checked connector toggles
+      modal.querySelectorAll('.connector-card').forEach(card => {
+        const checkbox = card.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"]');
+        const toggle = card.querySelector('.new-connector-toggle');
+        
+        if (checkbox && checkbox.checked && toggle) {
+          updateToggleState(toggle, newState);
+        }
+      });
+    });
+  }
+
+  // Wire up the "New Connection" button in the toolbar if it exists
+  const createBtn = document.getElementById('createBtn');
+  if (createBtn) {
+    createBtn.addEventListener('click', openNewConnectionModal);
+  }
+}
+
+// Initialize New Connection modal when DOM is ready
+document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', initNewConnectionModal);
+
 
   </script>

+            <div class="modal-header">

+                <button class="modal-close" onclick="closeModal('editValueModal')"><i class="fas fa-times"></i></button>

+    <script>
+        // Tab switching
+        document.querySelectorAll('.tab').forEach(tab => {
+            tab.addEventListener('click', function() {
+                const tabName = this.getAttribute('data-tab');
+                
+                document.querySelectorAll('.tab').forEach(t => t.classList.remove('active'));
+                document.querySelectorAll('.tab-content').forEach(c => c.classList.remove('active'));
+                
+                this.classList.add('active');
+                document.getElementById(tabName).classList.add('active');
+            });
+        });
+
+        // Modal functions
+        function openEditModal(fieldName, displayLabel, fieldType) {
+            document.getElementById('fieldName').value = fieldName;
+            document.getElementById('displayLabel').value = displayLabel;
+            document.getElementById('fieldType').value = fieldType.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + fieldType.slice(1);
+            document.getElementById('editFieldModal').classList.add('active');
+        }
+
+        function openHelpTextModal(fieldName, currentText) {
+            document.getElementById('helpFieldName').value = fieldName;
+            document.getElementById('helpText').value = currentText || '';
+            document.getElementById('helpTextModal').classList.add('active');
+        }
+
+        function openAddHelpTextModal() {
+            document.getElementById('newHelpFieldName').value = '';
+            document.getElementById('newHelpText').value = '';
+            document.getElementById('addHelpTextModal').classList.add('active');
+        }
+
+        function addNewHelpText() {
+            const fieldName = document.getElementById('newHelpFieldName').value;
+            const helpText = document.getElementById('newHelpText').value;
+            
+            if (!fieldName) {
+                showToast({ message: 'Please select a field', type: 'error', duration: 3000 });
+                return;
+            }
+            
+            if (!helpText.trim()) {
+                showToast({ message: 'Please enter help text', type: 'error', duration: 3000 });
+                return;
+            }
+            
+            // Add new row to table
+            const tbody = document.querySelector('#helpTextTable tbody');
+            const newRow = document.createElement('tr');
+            newRow.innerHTML = `
+                <td><span class="field-name">${fieldName}</span></td>
+                <td><span class="field-value">${helpText}</span></td>
+                <td>
+                    <div style="display: flex; gap: 8px;">
+                        <button class="btn btn-secondary btn-sm btn-icon" onclick="openHelpTextModal('${fieldName}', '${helpText.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}')"><i class="fas fa-edit"></i></button>
+                        <button class="btn btn-secondary btn-sm btn-icon" onclick="deleteHelpText('${fieldName}', this)"><i class="fas fa-trash"></i></button>
+                    </div>
+                </td>
+            `;
+            tbody.appendChild(newRow);
+            
+            showToast({ message: 'Help text added for: ' + fieldName, type: 'success', duration: 3000 });
+            closeModal('addHelpTextModal');
+        }
+
+        function deleteHelpText(fieldName, button) {
+            if (confirm('Are you sure you want to remove help text for "' + fieldName + '"?')) {
+                const row = button.closest('tr');
+                row.remove();
+                showToast({ message: 'Help text removed for: ' + fieldName, type: 'success', duration: 3000 });
+            }
+        }
+
+        function openAddValueModal(category) {
+            document.getElementById('addValueModal').classList.add('active');
+        }
+
+        function openSystemSettingModal(settingName) {
+            showToast({ message: 'Opening editor for: ' + settingName, type: 'info', title: 'System Setting Editor', duration: 3000 });
+        }
+
+        function closeModal(modalId) {
+            document.getElementById(modalId).classList.remove('active');
+        }
+
+        function saveFieldLabel() {
+            const label = document.getElementById('displayLabel').value;
+            showToast({ message: 'Field label updated to: ' + label, type: 'success', duration: 3000 });
+            closeModal('editFieldModal');
+        }
+
+        function saveHelpText() {
+            const text = document.getElementById('helpText').value;
+            showToast({ message: 'Help text has been updated', type: 'success', duration: 3000 });
+            closeModal('helpTextModal');
+        }
+
+        function addDropdownValue() {
+            const value = document.getElementById('newOptionValue').value;
+            if (value) {
+                showToast({ message: 'Added new option: ' + value, type: 'success', duration: 3000 });
+                closeModal('addValueModal');
+                document.getElementById('newOptionValue').value = '';
+            }
+        }
+
+        function editDropdownValue(value) {
+            document.getElementById('editOptionValue').value = value;
+            document.getElementById('editOptionOrder').value = 1;
+            document.getElementById('editValueModal').classList.add('active');
+        }
+
+        function saveEditedDropdownValue() {
+            const value = document.getElementById('editOptionValue').value;
+            if (value) {
+                showToast({ message: 'Updated option to: ' + value, type: 'success', duration: 3000 });
+                closeModal('editValueModal');
+            }
+        }
+
+        function deleteDropdownValue(value) {
+            if (confirm('Are you sure you want to delete "' + value + '"?')) {
+                showToast({ message: 'Option deleted: ' + value, type: 'success', duration: 3000 });
+            }
+        }
+
+        // Close modal on overlay click
+        document.querySelectorAll('.modal-overlay').forEach(overlay => {
+            overlay.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
+                if (e.target === this) {
+                    this.classList.remove('active');
+                }
+            });
+        });
+
+        // Header menu functionality
+        const menuButton = document.getElementById('menuButton');
+        const menuDropdown = document.getElementById('menuDropdown');
+        
+        menuButton.addEventListener('click', function() {
+            menuDropdown.classList.toggle('hidden');
+        });
+        
+        document.addEventListener('click', function(event) {
+            if (!menuButton.contains(event.target) && !menuDropdown.contains(event.target)) {
+                menuDropdown.classList.add('hidden');
+            }
+        });
+    </script>
+</body>
+</html>

+  <script>
+    document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item').forEach(item => {
+      item.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
+        const href = (this.getAttribute('href') || '').trim();
+        if (href === '' || href === '#') {
+          e.preventDefault();
+          document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item').forEach(nav => nav.classList.remove('active'));
+          this.classList.add('active');
+        }
+      });
+    });
+
+    // Close dropdowns when clicking outside
+    document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
+      if (menuDropdown) menuDropdown.classList.add('hidden');
+      if (notificationDropdown) notificationDropdown.classList.add('hidden');
+    });
+
+    // Modal functions
+    function openModal(id) {
+      document.getElementById(id).classList.add('active');
+      document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
+    }
+    function closeModal(id) {
+      document.getElementById(id).classList.remove('active');
+      document.body.style.overflow = '';
+    }
+
+    // Close modal on overlay click
+    document.querySelectorAll('.modal-overlay').forEach(overlay => {
+      overlay.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
+        if (e.target === this) closeModal(this.id);
+      });
+    });
+
+    // Permission toggle simulation
+    document.querySelectorAll('.permission-toggle').forEach(toggle => {
+      toggle.addEventListener('click', function() {
+        this.classList.toggle('active');
+      });
+    });
+
+    // Header menu functionality
+    const menuButton = document.getElementById('menuButton');
+    const menuDropdown = document.getElementById('menuDropdown');
+    const notificationButton = document.getElementById('notificationButton');
+    const notificationDropdown = document.getElementById('notificationDropdown');
+
+    if (menuButton && menuDropdown) {
+      menuButton.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
+        e.stopPropagation();
+        menuDropdown.classList.toggle('hidden');
+        if (notificationDropdown) notificationDropdown.classList.add('hidden');
+      });
+    }
+
+    if (notificationButton && notificationDropdown) {
+      notificationButton.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
+        e.stopPropagation();
+        notificationDropdown.classList.toggle('hidden');
+        if (menuDropdown) menuDropdown.classList.add('hidden');
+      });
+    }
+  </script>
+</body>
+</html>

+            <label class="permission-check-item"><input type="checkbox"><span class="permission-check-label">Create Users</span></label>
+            <label class="permission-check-item"><input type="checkbox" checked><span class="permission-check-label">View Campaigns</span></label>
+            <label class="permission-check-item"><input type="checkbox" checked><span class="permission-check-label">Create Campaigns</span></label>
+            <label class="permission-check-item"><input type="checkbox" checked><span class="permission-check-label">Edit Campaigns</span></label>

+  <script>
+    document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item').forEach(item => {
+      item.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
+        const href = (this.getAttribute('href') || '').trim();
+        if (href === '' || href === '#') {
+          e.preventDefault();
+          document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item').forEach(nav => nav.classList.remove('active'));
+          this.classList.add('active');
+        }
+      });
+    });
+
+    // Toggle members dropdown in table
+    function toggleMembersDropdown(button) {
+      const dropdown = button.closest('.members-dropdown');
+      const wasActive = dropdown.classList.contains('active');
+      
+      // Close all other dropdowns
+      document.querySelectorAll('.members-dropdown').forEach(d => d.classList.remove('active'));
+      
+      // Toggle this dropdown
+      if (!wasActive) {
+        dropdown.classList.add('active');
+      }
+    }
+
+    // Close dropdowns when clicking outside
+    document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
+      if (!e.target.closest('.members-dropdown')) {
+        document.querySelectorAll('.members-dropdown').forEach(d => d.classList.remove('active'));
+      }
+      if (menuDropdown) menuDropdown.classList.add('hidden');
+      if (notificationDropdown) notificationDropdown.classList.add('hidden');
+    });
+
+    // Modal functions
+    function openModal(id) {
+      document.getElementById(id).classList.add('active');
+      document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
+    }
+    function closeModal(id) {
+      document.getElementById(id).classList.remove('active');
+      document.body.style.overflow = '';
+    }
+
+    // Close modal on overlay click
+    document.querySelectorAll('.modal-overlay').forEach(overlay => {
+      overlay.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
+        if (e.target === this) closeModal(this.id);
+      });
+    });
+
+    // Permission toggle simulation
+    document.querySelectorAll('.permission-toggle').forEach(toggle => {
+      toggle.addEventListener('click', function() {
+        this.classList.toggle('active');
+      });
+    });
+
+    // Header menu functionality
+    const menuButton = document.getElementById('menuButton');
+    const menuDropdown = document.getElementById('menuDropdown');
+    const notificationButton = document.getElementById('notificationButton');
+    const notificationDropdown = document.getElementById('notificationDropdown');
+
+    if (menuButton && menuDropdown) {
+      menuButton.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
+        e.stopPropagation();
+        menuDropdown.classList.toggle('hidden');
+        if (notificationDropdown) notificationDropdown.classList.add('hidden');
+      });
+    }
+
+    if (notificationButton && notificationDropdown) {
+      notificationButton.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
+        e.stopPropagation();
+        notificationDropdown.classList.toggle('hidden');
+        if (menuDropdown) menuDropdown.classList.add('hidden');
+      });
+    }
+
+    // Role permissions configuration
+    const rolePermissions = {
+      'super-admin': {
+        name: 'Super Admin',
+        icon: 'super-admin',
+        iconClass: 'fa-crown',
+        permissions: ['view-users', 'create-users', 'edit-users', 'delete-users', 'assign-roles', 'view-activity', 
+                      'view-campaigns', 'create-campaigns', 'edit-campaigns', 'delete-campaigns', 'approve-campaigns',
+                      'view-reports', 'create-reports', 'export-reports', 'view-analytics',
+                      'view-billing', 'manage-billing', 'view-budgets', 'manage-budgets',
+                      'view-settings', 'manage-settings', 'manage-integrations']
+      },
+      'agency-admin': {
+        name: 'Agency Admin',
+        icon: 'agency-admin',
+        iconClass: 'fa-user-shield',
+        permissions: ['view-users', 'create-users', 'edit-users', 'assign-roles',
+                      'view-campaigns', 'create-campaigns', 'edit-campaigns', 'delete-campaigns', 'approve-campaigns',
+                      'view-reports', 'create-reports', 'export-reports',
+                      'view-billing', 'view-budgets']
+      },
+      'standard-user': {
+        name: 'Standard User',
+        icon: 'standard',
+        iconClass: 'fa-user',
+        permissions: ['view-users', 'view-campaigns', 'create-campaigns', 'edit-campaigns',
+                      'view-reports', 'export-reports']
+      },
+      'read-only': {
+        name: 'Read Only',
+        icon: 'read-only',
+        iconClass: 'fa-eye',
+        permissions: ['view-campaigns', 'view-reports']
+      },
+      'campaign-manager': {
+        name: 'Campaign Manager',
+        icon: 'custom',
+        iconClass: 'fa-cog',
+        permissions: ['view-users', 'view-campaigns', 'create-campaigns', 'edit-campaigns', 'delete-campaigns', 'approve-campaigns',
+                      'view-reports', 'create-reports', 'export-reports', 'view-budgets', 'manage-budgets']
+      }
+    };
+
+    // Open role permissions editor (switch to edit view)
+    function openRolePermissions(roleKey) {
+      const role = rolePermissions[roleKey];
+      if (!role) return;
+
+      // Update edit view header
+      document.getElementById('editRoleTitle').innerHTML = `Edit ${role.name} Permissions`;
+      document.getElementById('editRoleDescription').textContent = role.name;
+      const iconElement = document.getElementById('editRoleIcon');
+      iconElement.className = `role-icon ${role.icon}`;
+      iconElement.innerHTML = `<i class="fas ${role.iconClass}"></i>`;
+      iconElement.style.width = '32px';
+      iconElement.style.height = '32px';
+      iconElement.style.fontSize = '14px';
+
+      // Reset all checkboxes
+      document.querySelectorAll('.permission-checkbox').forEach(cb => cb.checked = false);
+
+      // Check permissions for this role
+      role.permissions.forEach(permissionKey => {
+        const permissionItem = document.querySelector(`[data-permission="${permissionKey}"]`);
+        if (permissionItem) {
+          const checkbox = permissionItem.querySelector('.permission-checkbox');
+          if (checkbox) checkbox.checked = true;
+        }
+      });
+
+      // Update counts
+      updatePermissionCount();
+
+      // Switch to edit view
+      showEditView();
+    }
+
+    // Toggle category collapse
+    function toggleCategory(header) {
+      header.classList.toggle('collapsed');
+    }
+
+    // Update permission counts
+    function updatePermissionCount() {
+      let totalSelected = 0;
+      
+      document.querySelectorAll('.permission-category').forEach(category => {
+        const checkboxes = category.querySelectorAll('.permission-checkbox');
+        const selectedInCategory = Array.from(checkboxes).filter(cb => cb.checked).length;
+        
+        const countSpan = category.querySelector('.selected-count');
+        if (countSpan) {
+          countSpan.textContent = selectedInCategory;
+        }
+        
+        totalSelected += selectedInCategory;
+      });
+      
+      const totalSpan = document.getElementById('totalSelectedPermissions');
+      if (totalSpan) {
+        totalSpan.textContent = totalSelected;
+      }
+    }
+
+    // Filter permissions by search
+    function filterPermissions(searchTerm) {
+      const term = searchTerm.toLowerCase();
+      
+      document.querySelectorAll('.permission-item').forEach(item => {
+        const name = item.querySelector('.permission-item-name').textContent.toLowerCase();
+        const desc = item.querySelector('.permission-item-desc').textContent.toLowerCase();
+        
+        if (name.includes(term) || desc.includes(term)) {
+          item.style.display = '';
+        } else {
+          item.style.display = 'none';
+        }
+      });
+
+      // Show/hide categories based on visible items
+      document.querySelectorAll('.permission-category').forEach(category => {
+        const visibleItems = Array.from(category.querySelectorAll('.permission-item'))
+          .filter(item => item.style.display !== 'none');
+        
+        if (visibleItems.length > 0 || term === '') {
+          category.style.display = '';
+        } else {
+          category.style.display = 'none';
+        }
+      });
+    }
+
+    // Save role permissions
+    function saveRolePermissions() {
+      // Get all selected permissions
+      const selectedPermissions = [];
+      document.querySelectorAll('.permission-checkbox:checked').forEach(cb => {
+        const item = cb.closest('.permission-item');
+        const permissionKey = item.getAttribute('data-permission');
+        selectedPermissions.push(permissionKey);
+      });
+
+      console.log('Saving permissions:', selectedPermissions);
+      
+      // Show success notification
+      showNotification('Role permissions updated successfully', 'success');
+      
+      // Return to roles view
+      showRolesView();
+    }
+
+    // Show edit view
+    function showEditView() {
+      document.getElementById('rolesContent').style.display = 'none';
+      document.getElementById('editRoleContent').style.display = 'block';
+      document.getElementById('mainHeader').style.display = 'none';
+      document.getElementById('editHeader').style.display = 'block';
+      document.getElementById('mainActions').style.display = 'none';
+      document.getElementById('editActions').style.display = 'block';
+    }
+
+    // Show roles view
+    function showRolesView() {
+      document.getElementById('rolesContent').style.display = 'block';
+      document.getElementById('editRoleContent').style.display = 'none';
+      document.getElementById('mainHeader').style.display = 'block';
+      document.getElementById('editHeader').style.display = 'none';
+      document.getElementById('mainActions').style.display = 'block';
+      document.getElementById('editActions').style.display = 'none';
+      
+      // Clear search
+      const searchInput = document.getElementById('permissionsSearchInput');
+      if (searchInput) searchInput.value = '';
+      filterPermissions('');
+    }
+
+    // Add click handlers to role rows to open permissions
+    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
+      // Make role rows clickable
+      const roleRows = document.querySelectorAll('.roles-table tbody tr');
+      roleRows.forEach((row, index) => {
+        const roleKeys = ['super-admin', 'agency-admin', 'standard-user', 'read-only', 'campaign-manager'];
+        row.style.cursor = 'pointer';
+        
+        row.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
+          // Don't trigger if clicking on action buttons or member dropdown
+          if (e.target.closest('.row-action') || e.target.closest('.members-count') || e.target.closest('.members-dropdown-content')) {
+            return;
+          }
+          
+          openRolePermissions(roleKeys[index]);
+        });
+      });
+    });
+  </script>
+</body>
+</html>

+    document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item').forEach(item => {
+      item.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
+        const href = (this.getAttribute('href') || '').trim();
+        if (href === '' || href === '#') {
+          e.preventDefault();
+          document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item').forEach(nav => nav.classList.remove('active'));
+          this.classList.add('active');
+        }
+      });
+    });
+
+    const searchInput = document.querySelector('.search-box input');
+    searchInput.addEventListener('focus', function() { this.parentElement.style.transform = 'scale(1.02)'; });
+    searchInput.addEventListener('blur', function() { this.parentElement.style.transform = 'scale(1)'; });
+  </script>
+  <script>
+    // Header menu functionality
+    const menuButton = document.getElementById('menuButton');
+    const menuDropdown = document.getElementById('menuDropdown');
+    const notificationButton = document.getElementById('notificationButton');
+    const notificationDropdown = document.getElementById('notificationDropdown');
+
+    if (menuButton && menuDropdown) {
+      menuButton.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
+        e.stopPropagation();
+        menuDropdown.classList.toggle('hidden');
+        if (notificationDropdown) notificationDropdown.classList.add('hidden');
+      });
+    }
+
+    if (notificationButton && notificationDropdown) {
+      notificationButton.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
+        e.stopPropagation();
+        notificationDropdown.classList.toggle('hidden');
+        if (menuDropdown) menuDropdown.classList.add('hidden');
+      });
+    }
+
+    document.addEventListener('click', function() {
+      if (menuDropdown) menuDropdown.classList.add('hidden');
+      if (notificationDropdown) notificationDropdown.classList.add('hidden');
+    });
+  </script>
+</body>

+
+  <script>
+    // Navigation
+    document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item').forEach(item => {
+      item.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
+        const href = (this.getAttribute('href') || '').trim();
+        if (href === '' || href === '#') {
+          e.preventDefault();
+          document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item').forEach(nav => nav.classList.remove('active'));
+          this.classList.add('active');
+        }
+      });
+    });
+
+    // Modal functions
+    function openModal(id) {
+      document.getElementById(id).classList.add('active');
+      document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
+    }
+    function closeModal(id) {
+      document.getElementById(id).classList.remove('active');
+      document.body.style.overflow = '';
+    }
+
+    // Close modal on overlay click
+    document.querySelectorAll('.modal-overlay').forEach(overlay => {
+      overlay.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
+        if (e.target === this) closeModal(this.id);
+      });
+    });
+
+    // Select all checkbox
+    document.getElementById('selectAll').addEventListener('change', function() {
+      document.querySelectorAll('#userTableBody .checkbox').forEach(cb => cb.checked = this.checked);
+    });
+
+    // Filter functionality
+    function clearFilters() {
+      document.getElementById('filterRole').value = '';
+      document.getElementById('filterSearch').value = '';
+    }
+
+    // Search animation (removed - no longer using .search-box)
+
+    // Header menu functionality
+    const menuButton = document.getElementById('menuButton');
+    const menuDropdown = document.getElementById('menuDropdown');
+    const notificationButton = document.getElementById('notificationButton');
+    const notificationDropdown = document.getElementById('notificationDropdown');
+
+    if (menuButton && menuDropdown) {
+      menuButton.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
+        e.stopPropagation();
+        menuDropdown.classList.toggle('hidden');
+        if (notificationDropdown) notificationDropdown.classList.add('hidden');
+      });
+    }
+
+    if (notificationButton && notificationDropdown) {
+      notificationButton.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
+        e.stopPropagation();
+        notificationDropdown.classList.toggle('hidden');
+        if (menuDropdown) menuDropdown.classList.add('hidden');
+      });
+    }
+
+    document.addEventListener('click', function() {
+      if (menuDropdown) menuDropdown.classList.add('hidden');
+      if (notificationDropdown) notificationDropdown.classList.add('hidden');
+    });
+
+    // Available roles data
+    const allRoles = [
+      {
+        id: 'super-admin',
+        name: 'Super Admin',
+        description: 'Full system access with all permissions',
+        icon: 'fas fa-crown',
+        iconClass: 'super-admin',
+        permissions: 47
+      },
+      {
+        id: 'agency-admin',
+        name: 'Agency Admin',
+        description: 'Manage agency users and campaigns',
+        icon: 'fas fa-user-tie',
+        iconClass: 'agency-admin',
+        permissions: 28
+      },
+      {
+        id: 'campaign-manager',
+        name: 'Campaign Manager',
+        description: 'Create and manage advertising campaigns',
+        icon: 'fas fa-bullhorn',
+        iconClass: 'campaign-manager',
+        permissions: 18
+      },
+      {
+        id: 'standard-user',
+        name: 'Standard User',
+        description: 'View and edit assigned campaigns',
+        icon: 'fas fa-user',
+        iconClass: 'standard-user',
+        permissions: 12
+      },
+      {
+        id: 'read-only',
+        name: 'Read Only',
+        description: 'View-only access to campaigns and reports',
+        icon: 'fas fa-eye',
+        iconClass: 'read-only',
+        permissions: 5
+      }
+    ];
+
+    // Current user's assigned roles
+    let currentUserRoles = [];
+
+    // View user details function
+    function viewUserDetails(name, email, initials, avatarGradient, assignedRoles) {
+      console.log('viewUserDetails called with:', { name, email, initials, avatarGradient, assignedRoles });
+      
+      // Hide users list view
+      document.getElementById('usersListView').style.display = 'none';
+      document.getElementById('mainHeader').style.display = 'none';
+      
+      // Show user details view
+      const userDetailsView = document.getElementById('userDetailsView');
+      console.log('userDetailsView element:', userDetailsView);
+      userDetailsView.classList.add('active');
+      userDetailsView.style.display = 'block'; // Force display
+      document.getElementById('userDetailsHeader').style.display = 'block';
+      
+      // Update user details header
+      document.getElementById('userDetailAvatar').textContent = initials;
+      document.getElementById('userDetailAvatar').style.background = avatarGradient;
+      document.getElementById('userDetailName').textContent = name;
+      document.getElementById('userDetailEmail').textContent = email;
+      
+      // Store current user's roles
+      currentUserRoles = assignedRoles || [];
+      console.log('Current user roles:', currentUserRoles);
+      
+      // Populate roles table
+      populateRolesTable();
+      
+      // Scroll to top
+      window.scrollTo(0, 0);
+    }
+
+    // Show users list view
+    function showUsersView() {
+      const userDetailsView = document.getElementById('userDetailsView');
+      userDetailsView.classList.remove('active');
+      userDetailsView.style.display = 'none'; // Explicitly hide
+      document.getElementById('userDetailsHeader').style.display = 'none';
+      document.getElementById('usersListView').style.display = 'block';
+      document.getElementById('mainHeader').style.display = 'block';
+    }
+
+    // Populate roles table
+    function populateRolesTable() {
+      const tbody = document.getElementById('rolesAssignmentBody');
+      tbody.innerHTML = '';
+      
+      allRoles.forEach(role => {
+        const isAssigned = currentUserRoles.includes(role.id);
+        
+        const row = document.createElement('tr');
+        row.innerHTML = `
+          <td style="text-align:center;">
+            <input type="checkbox" class="checkbox role-checkbox" data-role-id="${role.id}" ${isAssigned ? 'checked' : ''} onchange="updateAssignedRolesCount()">
+          </td>
+          <td>
+            <div class="role-name-cell">
+              <div class="role-icon-sm ${role.iconClass}">
+                <i class="${role.icon}"></i>
+              </div>
+              <div class="role-text-info">
+                <div class="role-title">${role.name}</div>
+                <div class="role-desc">${role.description}</div>
+              </div>
+            </div>
+          </td>
+          <td style="color:#64748b; font-size:13px;">${role.permissions} permissions</td>
+        `;
+        
+        tbody.appendChild(row);
+      });
+      
+      updateAssignedRolesCount();
+    }
+
+    // Update assigned roles count
+    function updateAssignedRolesCount() {
+      const checkedBoxes = document.querySelectorAll('.role-checkbox:checked');
+      document.getElementById('assignedRolesCount').textContent = checkedBoxes.length;
+    }
+
+    // Save user roles
+    function saveUserRoles() {
+      const checkedBoxes = document.querySelectorAll('.role-checkbox:checked');
+      const selectedRoles = Array.from(checkedBoxes).map(cb => cb.dataset.roleId);
+      
+      // Here you would normally save to backend
+      console.log('Saving roles:', selectedRoles);
+      
+      // Show success message (you can integrate with toast notification)
+      alert('User roles updated successfully!');
+      
+      // Return to users view
+      showUsersView();
+    }
+
+    // Delete user function (placeholder)
+    function deleteUser() {
+      if (confirm('Are you sure you want to delete this user? This action cannot be undone.')) {
+        console.log('Deleting user...');
+        alert('User deleted successfully!');
+        showUsersView();
+      }
+    }

+  function updateWizardUI() {
+    // Update step indicators
+    wizardSteps.forEach((step, index) => {
+      const stepNum = index + 1;
+      const stepNumber = step.querySelector('.step-number');
+      const stepTitle = step.querySelector('.step-title');
+
+      if (stepNum < currentStep) {
+        step.classList.add('completed');
+        step.classList.remove('active');
+        stepNumber.classList.remove('bg-blue-600', 'bg-gray-300');
+        stepNumber.classList.add('bg-green-500');
+      } else if (stepNum === currentStep) {
+        step.classList.add('active');
+        step.classList.remove('completed');
+        stepNumber.classList.remove('bg-gray-300', 'bg-green-500');
+        stepNumber.classList.add('bg-blue-600');
+      } else {
+        step.classList.remove('active', 'completed');
+        stepNumber.classList.remove('bg-blue-600', 'bg-green-500');
+        stepNumber.classList.add('bg-gray-300');
+      }
+    });
+
+    // Update content visibility
+    wizardContents.forEach((content, index) => {
+      if (index + 1 === currentStep) {
+        content.classList.add('active');
+      } else {
+        content.classList.remove('active');
+      }
+    });
+
+    // Update progress bar
+    const progress = (currentStep / totalSteps) * 100;
+    wizardProgressBar.style.width = `${progress}%`;
+    wizardProgressText.textContent = `${Math.round(progress)}%`;
+    wizardCurrentStep.textContent = currentStep;
+
+    // Update buttons
+    wizardPrevBtn.disabled = currentStep === 1;
+

+      wizardNextBtn.classList.add('hidden');

+    } else {
+      wizardNextBtn.classList.remove('hidden');

+    }

+  // Campaign Wizard Navigation Logic
+  let campaignCurrentStep = 1;
+  const campaignTotalSteps = 3;
+
+  function campaignWizardGoToStep(step) {
+    if (step < 1 || step > campaignTotalSteps) return;
+    
+    campaignCurrentStep = step;
+    
+    // Update step indicators
+    document.querySelectorAll('.wizard-step').forEach((stepEl, idx) => {
+      const stepNum = idx + 1;
+      const stepNumber = stepEl.querySelector('.step-number');
+      const stepTitle = stepEl.querySelector('.step-title');
+      
+      if (stepNum < campaignCurrentStep) {
+        // Completed steps
+        stepEl.classList.remove('active');
+        stepEl.classList.add('completed');
+        stepNumber?.classList.remove('bg-blue-600', 'bg-gray-300', 'text-gray-600');
+        stepNumber?.classList.add('bg-green-600', 'text-white');
+        stepTitle?.classList.remove('text-gray-600');
+        stepTitle?.classList.add('text-gray-900');
+      } else if (stepNum === campaignCurrentStep) {
+        // Active step
+        stepEl.classList.add('active');
+        stepEl.classList.remove('completed');
+        stepNumber?.classList.remove('bg-gray-300', 'bg-green-600', 'text-gray-600');
+        stepNumber?.classList.add('bg-blue-600', 'text-white');
+        stepTitle?.classList.remove('text-gray-600');
+        stepTitle?.classList.add('text-gray-900');
+      } else {
+        // Future steps
+        stepEl.classList.remove('active', 'completed');
+        stepNumber?.classList.remove('bg-blue-600', 'bg-green-600', 'text-white');
+        stepNumber?.classList.add('bg-gray-300', 'text-gray-600');
+        stepTitle?.classList.add('text-gray-600');
+        stepTitle?.classList.remove('text-gray-900');
+      }
+    });
+    
+    // Update content sections
+    document.querySelectorAll('.wizard-content').forEach((content, idx) => {
+      if (idx + 1 === campaignCurrentStep) {
+        content.classList.add('active');
+      } else {
+        content.classList.remove('active');
+      }
+    });
+    
+    // Update progress bar
+    const progressPercent = (campaignCurrentStep / campaignTotalSteps) * 100;
+    const progressBar = document.getElementById('campaignWizardProgressBar');
+    const progressText = document.getElementById('campaignWizardProgressText');
+    if (progressBar) progressBar.style.width = progressPercent + '%';
+    if (progressText) progressText.textContent = Math.round(progressPercent) + '%';
+    
+    // Update step counter
+    const currentStepEl = document.getElementById('campaignWizardCurrentStep');
+    if (currentStepEl) currentStepEl.textContent = campaignCurrentStep;
+    
+    // Update button states
+    const prevBtn = document.getElementById('campaignWizardPrevBtn');
+    const nextBtn = document.getElementById('campaignWizardNextBtn');
+    const createBtn = document.getElementById('campaignCreateBtn');
+    const createAndAddBtn = document.getElementById('createAndAddAdGroup');
+    
+    if (prevBtn) prevBtn.disabled = campaignCurrentStep === 1;
+    
+    if (campaignCurrentStep === campaignTotalSteps) {
+      // Last step - show create buttons
+      if (nextBtn) nextBtn.classList.add('hidden');
+      if (createBtn) createBtn.classList.remove('hidden');
+      if (createAndAddBtn) createAndAddBtn.classList.remove('hidden');
+    } else {
+      // Not last step - show next button
+      if (nextBtn) nextBtn.classList.remove('hidden');
+      if (createBtn) createBtn.classList.add('hidden');
+      if (createAndAddBtn) createAndAddBtn.classList.add('hidden');
+    }
+  }
+
+  // Wizard navigation buttons
+  document.getElementById('campaignWizardPrevBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
+    campaignWizardGoToStep(campaignCurrentStep - 1);
   });
 
+  document.getElementById('campaignWizardNextBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
+    campaignWizardGoToStep(campaignCurrentStep + 1);
+  });
+
+  // Allow clicking on steps to navigate (only to completed or active steps)
+  document.querySelectorAll('.wizard-step').forEach((stepEl, idx) => {
+    stepEl.addEventListener('click', () => {
+      const stepNum = idx + 1;
+      // Only allow going back to previous steps or current step
+      if (stepNum <= campaignCurrentStep) {
+        campaignWizardGoToStep(stepNum);
+      }
+    });
+  });
+

+// === WIZARD FUNCTIONALITY ===
+let currentStep = 1;
+const totalSteps = 3;
+
+function updateWizardUI() {
+  // Update step sidebar
+  document.querySelectorAll('.wizard-step').forEach(step => {
+    const stepNum = parseInt(step.dataset.step);
+    const stepNumber = step.querySelector('.step-number');
+    const stepTitle = step.querySelector('.step-title');
+    
+    if (stepNum < currentStep) {
+      // Completed step
+      step.classList.remove('active');
+      step.classList.add('completed');
+      stepNumber.classList.remove('bg-blue-600', 'bg-gray-300', 'text-gray-600');
+      stepNumber.classList.add('bg-green-600', 'text-white');
+      stepNumber.innerHTML = '✓';
+      stepTitle.classList.remove('text-gray-600');
+      stepTitle.classList.add('text-gray-900');
+    } else if (stepNum === currentStep) {
+      // Active step
+      step.classList.add('active');
+      step.classList.remove('completed');
+      stepNumber.classList.remove('bg-gray-300', 'bg-green-600', 'text-gray-600');
+      stepNumber.classList.add('bg-blue-600', 'text-white');
+      stepNumber.textContent = stepNum;
+      stepTitle.classList.remove('text-gray-600');
+      stepTitle.classList.add('text-gray-900');
+    } else {
+      // Upcoming step
+      step.classList.remove('active', 'completed');
+      stepNumber.classList.remove('bg-blue-600', 'bg-green-600', 'text-white');
+      stepNumber.classList.add('bg-gray-300', 'text-gray-600');
+      stepNumber.textContent = stepNum;
+      stepTitle.classList.add('text-gray-600');
+      stepTitle.classList.remove('text-gray-900');
+    }
+  });
+
+  // Update content visibility
+  document.querySelectorAll('.wizard-content').forEach(content => {
+    const contentNum = parseInt(content.dataset.content);
+    if (contentNum === currentStep) {
+      content.classList.add('active');
+    } else {
+      content.classList.remove('active');
+    }
+  });
+
+  // Update progress bar
+  const progressPercent = (currentStep / totalSteps) * 100;
+  document.getElementById('wizardProgressBar').style.width = progressPercent + '%';
+  document.getElementById('wizardProgressText').textContent = Math.round(progressPercent) + '%';
+  document.getElementById('wizardCurrentStep').textContent = currentStep;
+
+  // Update buttons
+  const prevBtn = document.getElementById('wizardPrevBtn');
+  const nextBtn = document.getElementById('wizardNextBtn');
+  const createBtn = document.getElementById('createAdGroupBtn');
+
+  prevBtn.disabled = currentStep === 1;
+  
+  if (currentStep === totalSteps) {
+    nextBtn.classList.add('hidden');
+    createBtn.classList.remove('hidden');
+  } else {
+    nextBtn.classList.remove('hidden');
+    createBtn.classList.add('hidden');
+  }
+
+  // Show/hide platform config sections based on selections
+  if (currentStep === 3) {
+    updatePlatformConfigVisibility();
+  }
+}

+function updatePlatformConfigVisibility() {
+  const dspCheckboxes = document.querySelectorAll('input[name="dsp"]:checked');
+  const adServerCheckboxes = document.querySelectorAll('input[name="adserver"]:checked');
+  
+  const dspSection = document.getElementById('dspFieldsSection');
+  const adServerSection = document.getElementById('adServerFieldsSection');
+  const noMessage = document.getElementById('noPlatformsMessage');
+  
+  const hasDSP = dspCheckboxes.length > 0;
+  const hasAdServer = adServerCheckboxes.length > 0;
+  
+  if (hasDSP || hasAdServer) {
+    noMessage.classList.add('hidden');
+    dspSection.classList.toggle('hidden', !hasDSP);
+    adServerSection.classList.toggle('hidden', !hasAdServer);
+  } else {
+    noMessage.classList.remove('hidden');
+    dspSection.classList.add('hidden');
+    adServerSection.classList.add('hidden');
+  }

+// Reset the Edit Connections Modal to default state
+function resetEditConnectionsModal() {
+  const modal = document.getElementById('editConnectionsModal');
+  if (!modal) return;
+
+  // Reset all checkboxes
+  modal.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]').forEach(cb => {
+    cb.checked = false;
+  });
+
+  // Reset all connector cards
+  modal.querySelectorAll('.connector-card').forEach(card => {
+    card.classList.remove('selected', 'border-blue-500', 'bg-blue-50');
+  });
+
+  // Reset all toggles
+  modal.querySelectorAll('.edit-connector-toggle').forEach(toggle => {
+    updateToggleState(toggle, false);
+  });
+
+  // Reset master toggle
+  const masterToggle = document.getElementById('editConnectorsToggle');
+  if (masterToggle) {
+    updateToggleState(masterToggle, false);
+  }
+}
+
+// Update toggle button state
+function updateToggleState(toggle, isEnabled) {
+  const span = toggle.querySelector('span[aria-hidden="true"]');
+  const statusLabel = toggle.closest('.connector-card')?.querySelector('.connector-status-label');
+  
+  if (isEnabled) {
+    toggle.classList.remove('bg-gray-200');
+    toggle.classList.add('bg-blue-600');
+    toggle.setAttribute('aria-checked', 'true');
+    if (span) {
+      span.classList.remove('translate-x-0');
+      span.classList.add('translate-x-5');
+    }
+    if (statusLabel) {
+      statusLabel.textContent = 'Synced';
+      statusLabel.classList.remove('text-gray-600');
+      statusLabel.classList.add('text-green-600');
+    }
+  } else {
+    toggle.classList.remove('bg-blue-600');
+    toggle.classList.add('bg-gray-200');
+    toggle.setAttribute('aria-checked', 'false');
+    if (span) {
+      span.classList.remove('translate-x-5');
+      span.classList.add('translate-x-0');
+    }
+    if (statusLabel) {
+      statusLabel.textContent = 'Not Synced';
+      statusLabel.classList.remove('text-green-600');
+      statusLabel.classList.add('text-gray-600');
+    }
+  }
+}
+
+// Close Edit Connections Modal
+function closeEditConnectionsModal() {
+  const modal = document.getElementById('editConnectionsModal');
+  if (modal) {
+    modal.classList.add('hidden');
+    modal.classList.remove('flex');
+  }
+}
+
+// Save Edit Connections
+function saveEditConnections() {
+  const modal = document.getElementById('editConnectionsModal');
+  if (!modal) return;
+
+  // Get current campaign
+  const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
+  const campaignId = urlParams.get('campaignId');
+  
+  if (!campaignId) {
+    if (window.toast && typeof window.toast.error === 'function') {
+      window.toast.error('Campaign ID not found');
+    }
+    return;
+  }
+
+  try {
+    const data = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('campaign_tree_groups') || '{}');
+    let campaign = null;
+    let campaigns = Array.isArray(data.campaigns) ? data.campaigns : [];
+    let groups = Array.isArray(data.groups) ? data.groups : [];
+
+    // Find the campaign
+    campaign = campaigns.find(c => c.id === campaignId);
+    
+    if (!campaign) {
+      for (const group of groups) {
+        if (group.campaigns) {
+          campaign = group.campaigns.find(c => c.id === campaignId);
+          if (campaign) break;
+        }
+      }
+    }
+
+    if (!campaign) {
+      if (window.toast && typeof window.toast.error === 'function') {
+        window.toast.error('Campaign not found');
+      }
+      return;
+    }
+
+    // Collect selected platforms and their status from the modal
+    const selectedDSP = [];
+    const selectedAdServer = [];
+    const connectionStatus = {};
+
+    modal.querySelectorAll('.connector-card').forEach(card => {
+      const checkbox = card.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"]');
+      const toggle = card.querySelector('.edit-connector-toggle');
+      
+      if (checkbox && checkbox.checked) {
+        const connectorType = checkbox.name; // 'edit-dsp' or 'edit-adserver'
+        const connectorValue = checkbox.value;
+        const isConnected = toggle && toggle.getAttribute('aria-checked') === 'true';
+        
+        if (connectorType === 'edit-dsp') {
+          selectedDSP.push(connectorValue);
+        } else if (connectorType === 'edit-adserver') {
+          selectedAdServer.push(connectorValue);
+        }
+        
+        connectionStatus[connectorValue] = isConnected ? 'Connected' : 'Disconnected';
+      }
+    });
+
+    // Update campaign connectors
+    campaign.connectors = {
+      dsp: selectedDSP,
+      adServer: selectedAdServer,
+      status: connectionStatus
+    };
+
+    // Save back to localStorage
+    localStorage.setItem('campaign_tree_groups', JSON.stringify(data));
+
+    // Show success message
+    if (window.toast && typeof window.toast.success === 'function') {
+      window.toast.success('Connections updated successfully');
+    }
+
+    // Close the modal
+    closeEditConnectionsModal();
+
+    // Reload the connections table
+    loadCampaignConnections(campaign);
+
+  } catch (error) {
+    console.error('Error saving connections:', error);
+    if (window.toast && typeof window.toast.error === 'function') {
+      window.toast.error('Failed to save connections');
+    }
+  }
+}
+
+// Initialize Edit Connections Modal event listeners
+function initEditConnectionsModal() {
+  const modal = document.getElementById('editConnectionsModal');
+  if (!modal) return;
+
+  // Close button
+  const closeBtn = document.getElementById('closeEditConnectionsModal');
+  if (closeBtn) {
+    closeBtn.addEventListener('click', closeEditConnectionsModal);
+  }
+
+  // Cancel button
+  const cancelBtn = document.getElementById('cancelEditConnections');
+  if (cancelBtn) {
+    cancelBtn.addEventListener('click', closeEditConnectionsModal);
+  }
+
+  // Save button
+  const saveBtn = document.getElementById('saveEditConnections');
+  if (saveBtn) {
+    saveBtn.addEventListener('click', saveEditConnections);
+  }
+
+  // Close on backdrop click
+  modal.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
+    if (e.target === modal) {
+      closeEditConnectionsModal();
+    }
+  });
+
+  // Connector card click handling (toggle checkbox)
+  modal.querySelectorAll('.connector-card').forEach(card => {
+    card.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
+      // Don't toggle if clicking on the checkbox, toggle button, or their children
+      if (e.target.closest('input[type="checkbox"]') || e.target.closest('.edit-connector-toggle')) {
+        return;
+      }
+      
+      const checkbox = card.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"]');
+      if (checkbox) {
+        checkbox.checked = !checkbox.checked;
+        
+        // Update card styling
+        if (checkbox.checked) {
+          card.classList.add('selected', 'border-blue-500', 'bg-blue-50');
+        } else {
+          card.classList.remove('selected', 'border-blue-500', 'bg-blue-50');
+        }
+      }
+    });
+  });
+
+  // Checkbox change handler
+  modal.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]').forEach(checkbox => {
+    checkbox.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
+      const card = checkbox.closest('.connector-card');
+      if (card) {
+        if (checkbox.checked) {
+          card.classList.add('selected', 'border-blue-500', 'bg-blue-50');
+        } else {
+          card.classList.remove('selected', 'border-blue-500', 'bg-blue-50');
+        }
+      }
+    });
+  });
+
+  // Individual connector toggle handling
+  modal.querySelectorAll('.edit-connector-toggle').forEach(toggle => {
+    toggle.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
+      e.stopPropagation();
+      const isCurrentlyEnabled = toggle.getAttribute('aria-checked') === 'true';
+      updateToggleState(toggle, !isCurrentlyEnabled);
+    });
+  });
+
+  // Master toggle handling
+  const masterToggle = document.getElementById('editConnectorsToggle');
+  if (masterToggle) {
+    masterToggle.addEventListener('click', () => {
+      const isCurrentlyEnabled = masterToggle.getAttribute('aria-checked') === 'true';
+      const newState = !isCurrentlyEnabled;
+      
+      // Update master toggle
+      updateToggleState(masterToggle, newState);
+      
+      // Update all checked connector toggles
+      modal.querySelectorAll('.connector-card').forEach(card => {
+        const checkbox = card.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"]');
+        const toggle = card.querySelector('.edit-connector-toggle');
+        
+        if (checkbox && checkbox.checked && toggle) {
+          updateToggleState(toggle, newState);
+        }
+      });
+    });
+  }
+}

+document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', initEditConnectionsModal);

+// ==================== NEW CONNECTION MODAL ====================

+// Open New Connection Modal
+function openNewConnectionModal() {
+  const modal = document.getElementById('newConnectionModal');
+  if (!modal) return;
+
+  // Reset all checkboxes and toggles first
+  resetNewConnectionModal();
+
+  // Show the modal
+  modal.classList.remove('hidden');
+  modal.classList.add('flex');
+}
+
+// Reset the New Connection Modal to default state
+function resetNewConnectionModal() {
+  const modal = document.getElementById('newConnectionModal');
+  if (!modal) return;
+
+  // Reset all checkboxes
+  modal.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]').forEach(cb => {
+    cb.checked = false;
+  });
+
+  // Reset all connector cards
+  modal.querySelectorAll('.connector-card').forEach(card => {
+    card.classList.remove('selected', 'border-blue-500', 'bg-blue-50');
+  });
+
+  // Reset all toggles
+  modal.querySelectorAll('.new-connector-toggle').forEach(toggle => {
+    updateToggleState(toggle, false);
+  });
+
+  // Reset master toggle
+  const masterToggle = document.getElementById('newConnectorsToggle');
+  if (masterToggle) {
+    updateToggleState(masterToggle, false);
+  }
+}
+
+// Close New Connection Modal
+function closeNewConnectionModal() {
+  const modal = document.getElementById('newConnectionModal');
+  if (modal) {
+    modal.classList.add('hidden');
+    modal.classList.remove('flex');
+  }
+}
+
+// Connect (Save) New Connections
+function connectNewConnections() {
+  const modal = document.getElementById('newConnectionModal');
+  if (!modal) return;
+
+  // Get current campaign
+  const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
+  const campaignId = urlParams.get('campaignId');
+  
+  if (!campaignId) {
+    if (window.toast && typeof window.toast.error === 'function') {
+      window.toast.error('Campaign ID not found');
+    }
+    return;
+  }
+
+  try {
+    const data = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('campaign_tree_groups') || '{}');
+    let campaign = null;
+    let campaigns = Array.isArray(data.campaigns) ? data.campaigns : [];
+    let groups = Array.isArray(data.groups) ? data.groups : [];
+
+    // Find the campaign
+    campaign = campaigns.find(c => c.id === campaignId);
+    
+    if (!campaign) {
+      for (const group of groups) {
+        if (group.campaigns) {
+          campaign = group.campaigns.find(c => c.id === campaignId);
+          if (campaign) break;
+        }
+      }
+    }
+
+    if (!campaign) {
+      if (window.toast && typeof window.toast.error === 'function') {
+        window.toast.error('Campaign not found');
+      }
+      return;
+    }
+
+    // Initialize connectors if not exists
+    if (!campaign.connectors) {
+      campaign.connectors = { dsp: [], adServer: [], status: {} };
+    }
+    if (!campaign.connectors.dsp) campaign.connectors.dsp = [];
+    if (!campaign.connectors.adServer) campaign.connectors.adServer = [];
+    if (!campaign.connectors.status) campaign.connectors.status = {};
+
+    // Collect selected platforms and their status from the modal
+    let newConnectionsAdded = 0;
+
+    modal.querySelectorAll('.connector-card').forEach(card => {
+      const checkbox = card.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"]');
+      const toggle = card.querySelector('.new-connector-toggle');
+      
+      if (checkbox && checkbox.checked) {
+        const connectorType = checkbox.name; // 'new-dsp' or 'new-adserver'
+        const connectorValue = checkbox.value;
+        const isConnected = toggle && toggle.getAttribute('aria-checked') === 'true';
+        
+        // Add to appropriate array if not already present
+        if (connectorType === 'new-dsp') {
+          if (!campaign.connectors.dsp.includes(connectorValue)) {
+            campaign.connectors.dsp.push(connectorValue);
+            newConnectionsAdded++;
+          }
+        } else if (connectorType === 'new-adserver') {
+          if (!campaign.connectors.adServer.includes(connectorValue)) {
+            campaign.connectors.adServer.push(connectorValue);
+            newConnectionsAdded++;
+          }
+        }
+        
+        // Update connection status
+        campaign.connectors.status[connectorValue] = isConnected ? 'Connected' : 'Disconnected';
+      }
+    });
+
+    if (newConnectionsAdded === 0) {
+      if (window.toast && typeof window.toast.info === 'function') {
+        window.toast.info('No new connections selected');
+      }
+      return;
+    }
+
+    // Save back to localStorage
+    localStorage.setItem('campaign_tree_groups', JSON.stringify(data));
+
+    // Show success message
+    if (window.toast && typeof window.toast.success === 'function') {
+      window.toast.success(`${newConnectionsAdded} connection(s) added successfully`);
+    }
+
+    // Close the modal
+    closeNewConnectionModal();
+
+    // Reload the connections table
+    loadCampaignConnections(campaign);
+
+  } catch (error) {
+    console.error('Error adding connections:', error);
+    if (window.toast && typeof window.toast.error === 'function') {
+      window.toast.error('Failed to add connections');
+    }
+  }
+}
+
+// Initialize New Connection Modal event listeners
+function initNewConnectionModal() {
+  const modal = document.getElementById('newConnectionModal');
+  if (!modal) return;
+
+  // Close button
+  const closeBtn = document.getElementById('closeNewConnectionModal');
+  if (closeBtn) {
+    closeBtn.addEventListener('click', closeNewConnectionModal);
+  }
+
+  // Cancel button
+  const cancelBtn = document.getElementById('cancelNewConnection');
+  if (cancelBtn) {
+    cancelBtn.addEventListener('click', closeNewConnectionModal);
+  }
+
+  // Connect button
+  const connectBtn = document.getElementById('connectNewConnection');
+  if (connectBtn) {
+    connectBtn.addEventListener('click', connectNewConnections);
+  }
+
+  // Close on backdrop click
+  modal.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
+    if (e.target === modal) {
+      closeNewConnectionModal();
+    }
+  });
+
+  // Connector card click handling (toggle checkbox)
+  modal.querySelectorAll('.connector-card').forEach(card => {
+    card.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
+      // Don't toggle if clicking on the checkbox, toggle button, or their children
+      if (e.target.closest('input[type="checkbox"]') || e.target.closest('.new-connector-toggle')) {
+        return;
+      }
+      
+      const checkbox = card.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"]');
+      if (checkbox) {
+        checkbox.checked = !checkbox.checked;
+        
+        // Update card styling
+        if (checkbox.checked) {
+          card.classList.add('selected', 'border-blue-500', 'bg-blue-50');
+        } else {
+          card.classList.remove('selected', 'border-blue-500', 'bg-blue-50');
+        }
+      }
+    });
+  });
+
+  // Checkbox change handler
+  modal.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]').forEach(checkbox => {
+    checkbox.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
+      const card = checkbox.closest('.connector-card');
+      if (card) {
+        if (checkbox.checked) {
+          card.classList.add('selected', 'border-blue-500', 'bg-blue-50');
+        } else {
+          card.classList.remove('selected', 'border-blue-500', 'bg-blue-50');
+        }
+      }
+    });
+  });
+
+  // Individual connector toggle handling
+  modal.querySelectorAll('.new-connector-toggle').forEach(toggle => {
+    toggle.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
+      e.stopPropagation();
+      const isCurrentlyEnabled = toggle.getAttribute('aria-checked') === 'true';
+      updateToggleState(toggle, !isCurrentlyEnabled);
+    });
+  });
+
+  // Master toggle handling
+  const masterToggle = document.getElementById('newConnectorsToggle');
+  if (masterToggle) {
+    masterToggle.addEventListener('click', () => {
+      const isCurrentlyEnabled = masterToggle.getAttribute('aria-checked') === 'true';
+      const newState = !isCurrentlyEnabled;
+      
+      // Update master toggle
+      updateToggleState(masterToggle, newState);
+      
+      // Update all checked connector toggles
+      modal.querySelectorAll('.connector-card').forEach(card => {
+        const checkbox = card.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"]');
+        const toggle = card.querySelector('.new-connector-toggle');
+        
+        if (checkbox && checkbox.checked && toggle) {
+          updateToggleState(toggle, newState);
+        }
+      });
+    });
+  }
+
+  // Wire up the "New Connection" button in the toolbar
+  const createBtn = document.getElementById('createBtn');
+  if (createBtn) {
+    createBtn.addEventListener('click', openNewConnectionModal);
+  }
+}

+document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', initNewConnectionModal);
