+      const acctEl = document.getElementById('advAccount');
+      const bcAdv  = document.getElementById('breadcrumbAdvertiser');
+      if (nameEl) nameEl.textContent = adv.name || 'Unknown';
+      if (acctEl) acctEl.textContent = adv.account || adv.accountNumber || '—';
+      if (bcAdv) {
+        bcAdv.textContent = adv.name || 'Unknown';
+        bcAdv.href = `./WFAdvertiserDetails.html?advertiserId=${adv.id}`;
+      }
+    }
+
+    if (!coId) {
+      document.getElementById('entitySections').innerHTML = '<p class="text-gray-500 text-center py-8">No change order specified.</p>';
+      return;
+    }
+
+    const co = getChangeOrder(coId);
+    if (!co) {
+      document.getElementById('entitySections').innerHTML = '<p class="text-gray-500 text-center py-8">Change order not found.</p>';
+      return;
+    }
+
+    // Populate header
+    document.getElementById('breadcrumbCOId').textContent = co.id;
+    document.getElementById('headerCOId').textContent = co.id;
+    document.getElementById('headerCreated').textContent = fmtDate(co.createdDate);
+    document.getElementById('headerOwner').textContent = co.owner || '—';
+    document.getElementById('coNameInput').value = co.name || '';
+    document.getElementById('generalNotes').value = co.generalNotes || '';
+
+    // Status badge
+    const badgeEl = document.getElementById('coStatusBadge');
+    const s = (co.status || 'draft').toLowerCase();
+    badgeEl.className = `co-badge co-badge-${s}`;
+    badgeEl.textContent = s.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + s.slice(1);
+
+    // Build entity sections
+    buildEntitySections(co);
+
+    // Wire up buttons
+    document.getElementById('saveCOBtn').addEventListener('click', () => {
+      co.name = document.getElementById('coNameInput').value.trim() || co.name;
+      co.generalNotes = document.getElementById('generalNotes').value;
+      co.modifiedDate = new Date().toISOString();
+
+      // Collect ad group field values
+      document.querySelectorAll('[data-ag-field]').forEach(input => {
+        const agId = input.dataset.agId;
+        const field = input.dataset.agField;
+        const entity = co.entities.find(e => e.type === 'adgroup' && e.id === agId);
+        if (entity) {
+          if (!entity.fields) entity.fields = {};
+          entity.fields[field] = input.value;
+        }
+      });
+
+      saveChangeOrder(co);
+      if (typeof showToast === 'function') showToast('Change order saved', 'success');
+    });
+
+    document.getElementById('syncCOBtn').addEventListener('click', () => {
+      co.status = 'synced';
+      co.modifiedDate = new Date().toISOString();
+      saveChangeOrder(co);
+      const badge = document.getElementById('coStatusBadge');
+      badge.className = 'co-badge co-badge-synced';
+      badge.textContent = 'Synced';
+      if (typeof showToast === 'function') showToast('Change order synced', 'success');
+    });
+
+    document.getElementById('exportCOBtn').addEventListener('click', () => {
+      const blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(co, null, 2)], { type: 'application/json' });
+      const a = document.createElement('a');
+      a.href = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
+      a.download = `${co.id}_${(co.name || 'export').replace(/\s+/g, '_')}.json`;
+      a.click();
+      URL.revokeObjectURL(a.href);
+      if (typeof showToast === 'function') showToast('Exported', 'success');
+    });
+
+    document.getElementById('manageEntitiesBtn').addEventListener('click', () => {
+      openEntitySelectModal(co.id);
+    });
+
+    // --- Helper functions ---
+
+    function fmtDate(d) {
+      if (!d) return '—';
+      try { return new Date(d).toLocaleDateString('en-US', { month: 'short', day: 'numeric', year: 'numeric' }); }
+      catch { return d; }
+    }
+
+    function entityPill(type) {
+      const map = {
+        advertiser: { label: 'ADV', bg: 'var(--brand-100, #dbeafe)', color: 'var(--brand-800, #014C86)' },
+        campaign:   { label: 'CAM', bg: '#e8e0f5', color: '#5a3d8a' },
+        adgroup:    { label: 'AG',  bg: '#fce8d5', color: '#8a5a2d' }
+      };
+      const p = map[type] || { label: type.toUpperCase(), bg: '#e5e7eb', color: '#374151' };
+      return `<span class="co-entity-pill" style="background:${p.bg};color:${p.color};">${p.label}</span>`;
+    }
+
+    function headerClass(type) {
+      const map = { advertiser: 'adv-header', campaign: 'cam-header', adgroup: 'ag-header' };
+      return map[type] || '';
+    }
+
+    function buildEntitySections(co) {
+      const container = document.getElementById('entitySections');
+      if (!co.entities || co.entities.length === 0) {
+        container.innerHTML = '<p class="text-gray-500 text-center py-8">No entities in this change order. Click "Manage Entities" to add some.</p>';
+        return;
+      }
+
+      container.innerHTML = '';
+
+      // Group: advertiser first, then campaigns, then ad groups
+      const order = ['advertiser', 'campaign', 'adgroup'];
+      const sorted = [...co.entities].sort((a, b) => order.indexOf(a.type) - order.indexOf(b.type));
+
+      sorted.forEach((entity, idx) => {
+        const secId = `sec-${entity.type}-${idx}`;
+        const isAdv = entity.type === 'advertiser';
+        const isAG  = entity.type === 'adgroup';
+
+        const section = document.createElement('div');
+        section.className = 'co-entity-section';
+        section.innerHTML = `
+          <div class="co-entity-header ${headerClass(entity.type)}" onclick="toggleSection('${secId}')">
+            <div class="entity-title">
+              <span class="toggle-arrow open" id="${secId}-arrow">▶</span>
+              ${entityPill(entity.type)}
+              ${entity.name || entity.id}
+            </div>
+            ${!isAdv ? `<span class="remove-btn" onclick="event.stopPropagation();removeEntity('${entity.type}','${entity.id}')">✕ Remove</span>` : ''}
+          </div>
+          <div class="co-entity-body" id="${secId}-body">
+            ${buildEntityBody(entity)}
+          </div>
+        `;
+        container.appendChild(section);
+      });
+    }
+
+    function buildEntityBody(entity) {
+      if (entity.type === 'advertiser') {
+        return `
+          <div class="flex gap-8 text-sm text-gray-600 mb-2">
+            <span><strong>Account #:</strong> ${adv ? (adv.account || adv.accountNumber || '—') : '—'}</span>
+            <span><strong>Name:</strong> ${entity.name || '—'}</span>
+          </div>
+          <p class="text-sm text-gray-400 italic">No changes requested at the advertiser level.</p>
+        `;
+      }
+
+      if (entity.type === 'campaign') {
+        // Look up campaign data  
+        let camData = {};
+        try {
+          const tree = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('campaign_tree_groups') || '{}');
+          let allCams = [];
+          if (tree.campaigns) allCams = allCams.concat(tree.campaigns);
+          if (tree.groups) tree.groups.forEach(g => { if (g.campaigns) allCams = allCams.concat(g.campaigns); });
+          camData = allCams.find(c => c.id === entity.id) || {};
+        } catch {}
+
+        return `
+          <div class="flex gap-8 text-sm text-gray-600 mb-2">
+            <span><strong>ID:</strong> ${entity.id}</span>
+            <span><strong>DSP:</strong> ${camData.dsp || '—'}</span>
+          </div>
+          <p class="text-sm text-gray-400 italic">No changes requested at the campaign level.</p>
+        `;
+      }
+
+      if (entity.type === 'adgroup') {
+        // Look up ad group data
+        let agData = {};
+        try {
+          const all = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('adgroups_data_v1') || '[]');
+          agData = all.find(a => a.id === entity.id) || {};
+        } catch {}
+
+        const fields = entity.fields || {};
+
+        return `
+          <div class="flex gap-8 text-sm text-gray-600 mb-4">
+            <span><strong>ID:</strong> ${entity.id}</span>
+            <span><strong>Classification:</strong> ${agData.classification || agData.multiviewClassification || '—'}</span>
+            <span><strong>Tactic:</strong> ${agData.multiviewTactic || '—'}</span>
+          </div>
+          <div class="co-fields-grid">
+            <div class="co-field-group">
+              <label>Start Date <span class="text-red-500 font-bold">*</span></label>
+              <input type="date" value="${fields.startDate || ''}" data-ag-id="${entity.id}" data-ag-field="startDate" class="w-full border border-gray-300 rounded-md px-2 py-1 text-sm required-field" />
+            </div>
+            <div class="co-field-group">
+              <label>End Date <span class="text-red-500 font-bold">*</span></label>
+              <input type="date" value="${fields.endDate || ''}" data-ag-id="${entity.id}" data-ag-field="endDate" class="w-full border border-gray-300 rounded-md px-2 py-1 text-sm required-field" />
+            </div>
+            <div class="co-field-group">
+              <label>Impressions <span class="text-red-500 font-bold">*</span></label>
+              <input type="text" value="${fields.impressions || ''}" placeholder="e.g. 500,000" data-ag-id="${entity.id}" data-ag-field="impressions" class="w-full border border-gray-300 rounded-md px-2 py-1 text-sm required-field" />
+            </div>
+            <div class="co-field-group">
+              <label>Monthly Impressions</label>
+              <input type="text" value="${fields.monthlyImpressions || ''}" placeholder="Optional" data-ag-id="${entity.id}" data-ag-field="monthlyImpressions" class="w-full border border-gray-300 rounded-md px-2 py-1 text-sm" />
+            </div>
+            <div class="co-field-group" style="grid-column: 1 / -1;">
+              <label>Additional Notes / Instructions</label>
+              <textarea data-ag-id="${entity.id}" data-ag-field="notes" class="w-full border border-gray-300 rounded-md px-2 py-1 text-sm" rows="3" placeholder="Targeting instructions, day parting, special requests...">${fields.notes || ''}</textarea>
+            </div>
+          </div>
+        `;
+      }
+
+      return '';
+    }
+
+    // Toggle section visibility
+    window.toggleSection = function(secId) {
+      const body = document.getElementById(secId + '-body');
+      const arrow = document.getElementById(secId + '-arrow');
+      if (body) body.classList.toggle('collapsed');
+      if (arrow) arrow.classList.toggle('open');
+    };
+
+    // Remove entity from CO
+    window.removeEntity = function(type, id) {
+      if (!confirm(`Remove this ${type} from the change order?`)) return;
+      co.entities = co.entities.filter(e => !(e.type === type && e.id === id));
+      co.modifiedDate = new Date().toISOString();
+      saveChangeOrder(co);
+      buildEntitySections(co);
+      if (typeof showToast === 'function') showToast(`${type} removed`, 'info');
+    };
+
+    // Waffle menu toggle
+    const menuBtn = document.getElementById('menuButton');
+    const menuDrop = document.getElementById('menuDropdown');
+    if (menuBtn && menuDrop) {
+      menuBtn.addEventListener('click', () => menuDrop.classList.toggle('hidden'));
+      document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
+        if (!menuBtn.contains(e.target) && !menuDrop.contains(e.target)) menuDrop.classList.add('hidden');
+      });
+    }
+  });
+  </script>
+
+  <script src="./assets/sidebar.js" defer></script>
+</body>
+</html>

+            <div>
+              <h1 id="advName" class="md:text-2xl font-semibold text-gray-900">Loading…</h1>
+              <h3 class="text-sm font-semibold text-gray-600">Account #: <span id="advAccount" class="text-sm text-gray-500">—</span></h3>
+            </div>
+            <div class="text-right">
+              <div class="flex justify-end gap-2">
+                <span class="text-sm font-semibold text-gray-600">ID:</span>
+                <span id="advId" class="text-sm text-gray-500 w-28 text-left">—</span>
+              </div>
+            </div>
+          </div>
+
+          <hr class="border-gray-300 mp-4 p-2">
+
+          <!-- Section Title -->
+          <section>
+            <div class="flex items-center justify-between mb-6">
+              <h1 class="text-2xl font-semibold text-gray-900 mx-2">CHANGE ORDERS</h1>
+            </div>
+
+            <!-- Toolbar -->
+            <div class="flex items-center gap-3 mb-4 px-2">
+              <button id="newCOBtn" onclick="openCOPickerModal()" class="flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2 text-sm bg-green-600 text-white border border-green-600 rounded-md hover:bg-green-700 transition-colors" title="New Change Order">
+                <svg class="w-4 h-4" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M12 4v16m8-8H4"/></svg>
+                <span>New Change Order</span>
+              </button>
+              <div class="h-6 w-px bg-gray-300"></div>
+              <select id="statusFilter" class="text-sm border border-gray-300 rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-gray-700 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500 focus:border-blue-500">
+                <option value="draft,synced" selected>Draft &amp; Synced</option>
+                <option value="all">All Statuses</option>
+                <option value="draft">Draft</option>
+                <option value="synced">Synced</option>
+                <option value="active">Active</option>
+                <option value="cancelled">Cancelled</option>
+              </select>
+              <input id="searchInput" type="text" placeholder="Search..." class="text-sm border border-gray-300 rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-gray-700 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500 focus:border-blue-500 w-48" />
+              <span id="coCount" class="text-sm text-gray-500 ml-auto"></span>
+            </div>

+                  <col style="width: 10%;">
+                </colgroup>
+                <thead class="tbl-head">
+                  <tr>
+                    <th scope="col" class="text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 uppercase tracking-wider border-r border-gray-200">
+                      <button type="button" class="sort-btn flex w-full items-center px-4 py-2 space-x-2" data-sort-key="id">
+                        <span>ID</span>

+                        <span>Modified</span>
+                      </button>

+                    <th scope="col" class="text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 uppercase tracking-wider border-r border-gray-200">

+                        <span>Owner</span>

+                      <button type="button" class="sort-btn flex w-full items-center px-4 py-2 space-x-2" data-sort-key="campaigns">
+                        <span>Campaigns</span>
+                      </button>
+                    </th>
+                    <th scope="col" class="text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 uppercase tracking-wider border-r border-gray-200">
+                      <button type="button" class="sort-btn flex w-full items-center px-4 py-2 space-x-2" data-sort-key="adGroups">
+                        <span>Ad Groups</span>

+  <!-- Page Script -->
+  <script>
+  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
+    // Load advertiser info
+    let adv = null;
+    try {
+      const raw = localStorage.getItem('adv_selected_data');
+      if (raw) adv = JSON.parse(raw);
+    } catch {}
+
+    if (adv) {
+      const nameEl = document.getElementById('advName');
+      const acctEl = document.getElementById('advAccount');
+      const idEl   = document.getElementById('advId');
+      const bcAdv  = document.getElementById('breadcrumbAdvertiser');
+      if (nameEl) nameEl.textContent = adv.name || 'Unknown';
+      if (acctEl) acctEl.textContent = adv.account || adv.accountNumber || '—';
+      if (idEl)   idEl.textContent   = adv.id || '—';
+      if (bcAdv) {
+        bcAdv.textContent = adv.name || 'Unknown';
+        bcAdv.href = `./WFAdvertiserDetails.html?advertiserId=${adv.id}`;
+      }
+    }
+
+    // Status badge helper
+    function statusBadge(status) {
+      const s = (status || 'draft').toLowerCase();
+      return `<span class="co-badge co-badge-${s}">${s.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + s.slice(1)}</span>`;
+    }
+
+    // Format date helper
+    function fmtDate(d) {
+      if (!d) return '—';
+      try {
+        return new Date(d).toLocaleDateString('en-US', { month: 'short', day: 'numeric', year: 'numeric' });
+      } catch { return d; }
+    }
+
+    // Count entities helper
+    function countEntities(entities, type) {
+      if (!entities || !Array.isArray(entities)) return 0;
+      return entities.filter(e => e.type === type).length;
+    }
+
+    // Render table
+    function renderTable() {
+      const tbody = document.getElementById('coTableBody');
+      const countEl = document.getElementById('coCount');
+      if (!tbody) return;
+
+      const allCOs = getChangeOrders();
+      const filterVal = document.getElementById('statusFilter').value;
+      const searchVal = (document.getElementById('searchInput').value || '').toLowerCase();
+
+      // Filter by status
+      let filtered = allCOs;
+      if (filterVal !== 'all') {
+        const allowed = filterVal.split(',');
+        filtered = filtered.filter(co => allowed.includes((co.status || 'draft').toLowerCase()));
+      }
+
+      // Filter by search
+      if (searchVal) {
+        filtered = filtered.filter(co =>
+          (co.id || '').toLowerCase().includes(searchVal) ||
+          (co.name || '').toLowerCase().includes(searchVal) ||
+          (co.owner || '').toLowerCase().includes(searchVal)
+        );
+      }
+
+      // Sort by modified date descending
+      filtered.sort((a, b) => new Date(b.modifiedDate || 0) - new Date(a.modifiedDate || 0));
+
+      const hiddenCount = allCOs.length - filtered.length;
+
+      if (filtered.length === 0) {
+        tbody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="9" class="px-6 py-8 text-center text-gray-500">No change orders found</td></tr>';
+        if (countEl) countEl.textContent = allCOs.length === 0 ? '' : `0 showing (${hiddenCount} hidden by filter)`;
+        return;
+      }
+
+      tbody.innerHTML = '';
+      filtered.forEach(co => {
+        const camCount = countEntities(co.entities, 'campaign');
+        const agCount  = countEntities(co.entities, 'adgroup');
+        const canDelete = (co.status || 'draft').toLowerCase() !== 'synced';
+
+        const tr = document.createElement('tr');
+        tr.className = 'hover:bg-gray-50';
+        tr.innerHTML = `
+          <td class="px-4 py-1 whitespace-nowrap text-sm border-r border-default">
+            <a href="./ChangeOrderDetail.html?coId=${encodeURIComponent(co.id)}" class="text-blue-600 hover:underline">${co.id}</a>
+          </td>
+          <td class="px-4 py-1 whitespace-nowrap text-sm font-medium border-r border-default">${co.name || '—'}</td>
+          <td class="px-4 py-1 whitespace-nowrap text-sm border-r border-default">${statusBadge(co.status)}</td>
+          <td class="px-4 py-1 whitespace-nowrap text-sm border-r border-default">${fmtDate(co.modifiedDate)}</td>
+          <td class="px-4 py-1 whitespace-nowrap text-sm border-r border-default">${fmtDate(co.createdDate)}</td>
+          <td class="px-4 py-1 whitespace-nowrap text-sm border-r border-default">${co.owner || '—'}</td>
+          <td class="px-4 py-1 whitespace-nowrap text-sm text-right border-r border-default">${camCount}</td>
+          <td class="px-4 py-1 whitespace-nowrap text-sm text-right border-r border-default">${agCount}</td>
+          <td class="px-4 py-1 whitespace-nowrap text-sm">
+            <a href="./ChangeOrderDetail.html?coId=${encodeURIComponent(co.id)}" class="text-blue-600 hover:underline mr-2">View</a>
+            <span class="text-blue-600 hover:underline cursor-pointer mr-2" onclick="exportCO('${co.id}')">Export</span>
+            ${canDelete ? `<span class="text-red-600 hover:underline cursor-pointer" onclick="deleteCORow('${co.id}')">Delete</span>` : ''}
+          </td>
+        `;
+        tbody.appendChild(tr);
+      });
+
+      if (countEl) {
+        countEl.textContent = `${filtered.length} change order${filtered.length !== 1 ? 's' : ''} showing` +
+          (hiddenCount > 0 ? ` (${hiddenCount} hidden)` : '');
+      }
+    }
+
+    // Wire up filter and search
+    document.getElementById('statusFilter').addEventListener('change', renderTable);
+    document.getElementById('searchInput').addEventListener('input', renderTable);
+
+    // Expose helpers globally
+    window.deleteCORow = function(id) {
+      if (confirm('Delete this change order? This cannot be undone.')) {
+        deleteChangeOrder(id);
+        renderTable();
+        if (typeof showToast === 'function') showToast('Change order deleted', 'success');
+      }
+    };
+
+    window.exportCO = function(id) {
+      const co = getChangeOrder(id);
+      if (!co) return;
+      const blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(co, null, 2)], { type: 'application/json' });
+      const a = document.createElement('a');
+      a.href = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
+      a.download = `${co.id}_${(co.name || 'export').replace(/\s+/g, '_')}.json`;
+      a.click();
+      URL.revokeObjectURL(a.href);
+      if (typeof showToast === 'function') showToast('Change order exported', 'success');
+    };
+
+    // Initial render
+    renderTable();
+
+    // Re-render on storage changes
+    window.addEventListener('storage', (e) => {
+      if (e.key === 'change_orders_data') renderTable();
+    });
+
+    // Waffle menu toggle
+    const menuBtn = document.getElementById('menuButton');
+    const menuDrop = document.getElementById('menuDropdown');
+    if (menuBtn && menuDrop) {
+      menuBtn.addEventListener('click', () => menuDrop.classList.toggle('hidden'));
+      document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
+        if (!menuBtn.contains(e.target) && !menuDrop.contains(e.target)) menuDrop.classList.add('hidden');
+      });
+    }
+  });
+  </script>
+
+  <script src="./assets/sidebar.js" defer></script>
+</body>
+</html>

+    <script>
+        // Add some basic interactivity
+        document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item').forEach(item => {
+            item.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
+                const href = (this.getAttribute('href') || '').trim();
+
+                // Keep the "active" behavior for placeholder links, but allow real links to navigate.
+                if (href === '' || href === '#') {
+                    e.preventDefault();
+                    document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item').forEach(nav => nav.classList.remove('active'));
+                    this.classList.add('active');
+                }
+            });
+        });
+
+        // Search functionality
+        const searchInput = document.querySelector('.search-box input');
+        searchInput.addEventListener('focus', function() {
+            this.parentElement.style.transform = 'scale(1.02)';
+        });
+        
+        searchInput.addEventListener('blur', function() {
+            this.parentElement.style.transform = 'scale(1)';
+        });
+
+        // Simulate real-time updates
+        function updateStats() {
+            const statValues = document.querySelectorAll('.stat-value');
+            statValues.forEach(stat => {
+                // Add subtle animation on data updates
+                stat.style.transform = 'scale(1.05)';
+                setTimeout(() => {
+                    stat.style.transform = 'scale(1)';
+                }, 200);
+            });
+        }
+
+        // Update stats every 30 seconds to show it's "live"
+        setInterval(updateStats, 30000);
+    </script>

+        buildPlatformsFromConnectors: function(advertiser) {
+          const platforms = [];
+          const now = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 19).replace('T', ' ');
+          
+          // Platform configuration mapping
+          const platformConfig = {
+            'trade-desk': {
+              name: 'The Trade Desk',
+              type: 'DSP'
+            },
+            'dv360': {
+              name: 'Display & Video 360',
+              type: 'DSP'
+            },
+            'simplifi': {
+              name: 'Simplifi',
+              type: 'DSP'
+            },
+            'google-campaign-manager': {
+              name: 'Google Campaign Manager',
+              type: 'Ad Server'
+            }
+          };
+          
+          // Process DSP platforms
+          if (advertiser.connectors.dsp && Array.isArray(advertiser.connectors.dsp)) {
+            advertiser.connectors.dsp.forEach(dspValue => {
+              if (platformConfig[dspValue]) {
+                const status = advertiser.connectors.status && advertiser.connectors.status[dspValue]
+                  ? (advertiser.connectors.status[dspValue] === 'Connected' ? 'ENABLED' : 'DISABLED')
+                  : 'ENABLED';
+                
+                platforms.push({
+                  platform: platformConfig[dspValue].name,
+                  platformType: platformConfig[dspValue].type,
+                  status: status,
+                  enabled_at: status === 'ENABLED' ? now : '—',
+                  disabled_at: status === 'DISABLED' ? now : null
+                });
+              }
+            });
+          }
+          
+          // Process Ad Server platforms
+          if (advertiser.connectors.adServer && Array.isArray(advertiser.connectors.adServer)) {
+            advertiser.connectors.adServer.forEach(adServerValue => {
+              if (platformConfig[adServerValue]) {
+                const status = advertiser.connectors.status && advertiser.connectors.status[adServerValue]
+                  ? (advertiser.connectors.status[adServerValue] === 'Connected' ? 'ENABLED' : 'DISABLED')
+                  : 'ENABLED';
+                
+                platforms.push({
+                  platform: platformConfig[adServerValue].name,
+                  platformType: platformConfig[adServerValue].type,
+                  status: status,
+                  enabled_at: status === 'ENABLED' ? now : '—',
+                  disabled_at: status === 'DISABLED' ? now : null
+                });
+              }
+            });
+          }
+          
+          return platforms.length > 0 ? platforms : [...DEFAULT_ADGROUPS];
+        },

+    // ==================== EDIT CONNECTIONS MODAL ====================
+
+    // Open Edit Connections Modal
+    // platformTypeFilter: 'DSP', 'Ad Server', or null (show all)
+    function openEditConnectionsModal(platformTypeFilter) {
+      const modal = document.getElementById('editConnectionsModal');
+      if (!modal) return;
+
+      // Reset all checkboxes and toggles first
+      resetEditConnectionsModal();
+
+      // Show/hide sections based on platform type filter
+      const dspSection = document.getElementById('editDspSection');
+      const adServerSection = document.getElementById('editAdServerSection');
+      
+      // Get all DSP connector cards
+      const dspCards = modal.querySelectorAll('.connector-card[data-connector="trade-desk"], .connector-card[data-connector="dv360"], .connector-card[data-connector="simplifi"]');
+      // Get all Ad Server connector cards
+      const adServerCards = modal.querySelectorAll('.connector-card[data-connector="google-campaign-manager"]');
+      
+      if (platformTypeFilter === 'DSP') {
+        // Show only DSP section
+        if (dspSection) dspSection.style.display = '';
+        dspCards.forEach(card => card.style.display = '');
+        if (adServerSection) adServerSection.style.display = 'none';
+        adServerCards.forEach(card => card.style.display = 'none');
+      } else if (platformTypeFilter === 'Ad Server') {
+        // Show only Ad Server section
+        if (dspSection) dspSection.style.display = 'none';
+        dspCards.forEach(card => card.style.display = 'none');
+        if (adServerSection) adServerSection.style.display = '';
+        adServerCards.forEach(card => card.style.display = '');
+      } else {
+        // Show all sections (no filter)
+        if (dspSection) dspSection.style.display = '';
+        dspCards.forEach(card => card.style.display = '');
+        if (adServerSection) adServerSection.style.display = '';
+        adServerCards.forEach(card => card.style.display = '');
+      }
+
+      // Read current connections from the table
+      const tableBody = document.getElementById('campaignTableBody');
+      if (tableBody) {
+        const rows = tableBody.querySelectorAll('tr');
+        
+        rows.forEach(row => {
+          const platformCell = row.querySelector('td:nth-child(1)');
+          const platformTypeCell = row.querySelector('td:nth-child(2)');
+          const platformName = platformCell ? platformCell.textContent.trim() : '';
+          const platformType = platformTypeCell ? platformTypeCell.textContent.trim() : '';
+          
+          // Map platform name to connector value
+          const platformMap = {
+            'The Trade Desk': 'trade-desk',
+            'DV360': 'dv360',
+            'Display & Video 360': 'dv360',
+            'Simplifi': 'simplifi',
+            'Google Campaign Manager': 'google-campaign-manager'
+          };
+          
+          const platformValue = platformMap[platformName];
+          if (!platformValue) return;
+          
+          // Check if this platform is in the table (enabled)
+          const checkbox = modal.querySelector(`input[value="${platformValue}"]`);
+          if (checkbox) {
+            checkbox.checked = true;
+            
+            // Update the card styling
+            const card = checkbox.closest('.connector-card');
+            if (card) {
+              card.classList.add('selected', 'border-blue-500', 'bg-blue-50');
+            }
+            
+            // Find if this row is connected (ENABLED status)
+            // Look for "Create" link - if present, it's disconnected
+            const createLink = row.querySelector('a[data-action="create-connection"]');
+            const isConnected = !createLink;
+            
+            // Find the toggle button for this connector
+            const toggle = modal.querySelector(`.edit-connector-toggle[data-connector="${platformValue}"]`);
+            if (toggle) {
+              updateToggleState(toggle, isConnected);
+            }
+          }
+        });
+      }
+
+      // Show the modal
+      modal.classList.remove('hidden');
+      modal.classList.add('flex');
+    }
+
+    // Reset the Edit Connections Modal to default state
+    function resetEditConnectionsModal() {
+      const modal = document.getElementById('editConnectionsModal');
+      if (!modal) return;
+
+      // Reset all checkboxes
+      modal.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]').forEach(cb => {
+        cb.checked = false;
+      });
+
+      // Reset all connector cards
+      modal.querySelectorAll('.connector-card').forEach(card => {
+        card.classList.remove('selected', 'border-blue-500', 'bg-blue-50');
+      });
+
+      // Reset all toggles
+      modal.querySelectorAll('.edit-connector-toggle').forEach(toggle => {
+        updateToggleState(toggle, false);
+      });
+
+      // Reset master toggle
+      const masterToggle = document.getElementById('editConnectorsToggle');
+      if (masterToggle) {
+        updateToggleState(masterToggle, false);
+      }
+    }
+
+    // Update toggle button state
+    function updateToggleState(toggle, isEnabled) {
+      const span = toggle.querySelector('span[aria-hidden="true"]');
+      const statusLabel = toggle.closest('.connector-card')?.querySelector('.connector-status-label');
+      
+      if (isEnabled) {
+        toggle.classList.remove('bg-gray-200');
+        toggle.classList.add('bg-blue-600');
+        toggle.setAttribute('aria-checked', 'true');
+        if (span) {
+          span.classList.remove('translate-x-0');
+          span.classList.add('translate-x-5');
+        }
+        if (statusLabel) {
+          statusLabel.textContent = 'Synced';
+          statusLabel.classList.remove('text-gray-600');
+          statusLabel.classList.add('text-green-600');
+        }
+      } else {
+        toggle.classList.remove('bg-blue-600');
+        toggle.classList.add('bg-gray-200');
+        toggle.setAttribute('aria-checked', 'false');
+        if (span) {
+          span.classList.remove('translate-x-5');
+          span.classList.add('translate-x-0');
+        }
+        if (statusLabel) {
+          statusLabel.textContent = 'Not Synced';
+          statusLabel.classList.remove('text-green-600');
+          statusLabel.classList.add('text-gray-600');
+        }
+      }
+    }
+
+    // Close Edit Connections Modal
+    function closeEditConnectionsModal() {
+      const modal = document.getElementById('editConnectionsModal');
+      if (modal) {
+        modal.classList.add('hidden');
+        modal.classList.remove('flex');
+      }
+    }
+
+    // Save Edit Connections
+    function saveEditConnections() {
+      const modal = document.getElementById('editConnectionsModal');
+      if (!modal) return;
+
+      try {
+        // Get advertiser data
+        let advertiser = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('adv_selected_data') || '{}');
+        
+        if (!advertiser.id) {
+          if (window.toast && typeof window.toast.error === 'function') {
+            window.toast.error('Advertiser data not found');
+          }
+          return;
+        }
+
+        // Collect selected platforms and their status from the modal
+        const selectedDSP = [];
+        const selectedAdServer = [];
+        const connectionStatus = {};
+
+        modal.querySelectorAll('.connector-card').forEach(card => {
+          const checkbox = card.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"]');
+          const toggle = card.querySelector('.edit-connector-toggle');
+          
+          if (checkbox && checkbox.checked) {
+            const connectorType = checkbox.name; // 'edit-dsp' or 'edit-adserver'
+            const connectorValue = checkbox.value;
+            const isConnected = toggle && toggle.getAttribute('aria-checked') === 'true';
+            
+            if (connectorType === 'edit-dsp') {
+              selectedDSP.push(connectorValue);
+            } else if (connectorType === 'edit-adserver') {
+              selectedAdServer.push(connectorValue);
+            }
+            
+            connectionStatus[connectorValue] = isConnected ? 'Connected' : 'Disconnected';
+          }
+        });
+
+        // Update advertiser connectors
+        advertiser.connectors = {
+          dsp: selectedDSP,
+          adServer: selectedAdServer,
+          status: connectionStatus
+        };
+
+        // Save back to localStorage
+        localStorage.setItem('adv_selected_data', JSON.stringify(advertiser));
+
+        // Rebuild the connections table from the updated connectors
+        if (app) {
+          app.adgroups = app.buildPlatformsFromConnectors(advertiser);
+          app.saveAdGroups();
+          app.applyFiltersAndRender();
+        }
+
+        // Show success message
+        if (window.toast && typeof window.toast.success === 'function') {
+          window.toast.success('Connections updated successfully');
+        }
+
+        // Close the modal
+        closeEditConnectionsModal();
+
+      } catch (error) {
+        console.error('Error saving connections:', error);
+        if (window.toast && typeof window.toast.error === 'function') {
+          window.toast.error('Failed to save connections');
+        }
+      }
+    }
+
+    // Initialize Edit Connections Modal event listeners
+    function initEditConnectionsModal() {
+      const modal = document.getElementById('editConnectionsModal');
+      if (!modal) return;
+
+      // Close button
+      const closeBtn = document.getElementById('closeEditConnectionsModal');
+      if (closeBtn) {
+        closeBtn.addEventListener('click', closeEditConnectionsModal);
+      }
+
+      // Cancel button
+      const cancelBtn = document.getElementById('cancelEditConnections');
+      if (cancelBtn) {
+        cancelBtn.addEventListener('click', closeEditConnectionsModal);
+      }
+
+      // Save button
+      const saveBtn = document.getElementById('saveEditConnections');
+      if (saveBtn) {
+        saveBtn.addEventListener('click', saveEditConnections);
+      }
+
+      // Close on backdrop click
+      modal.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
+        if (e.target === modal) {
+          closeEditConnectionsModal();
+        }
+      });
+
+      // Connector card click handling (toggle checkbox)
+      modal.querySelectorAll('.connector-card').forEach(card => {
+        card.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
+          // Don't toggle if clicking on the checkbox, toggle button, or their children
+          if (e.target.closest('input[type="checkbox"]') || e.target.closest('.edit-connector-toggle')) {
+            return;
+          }
+          
+          const checkbox = card.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"]');
+          if (checkbox) {
+            checkbox.checked = !checkbox.checked;
+            
+            // Update card styling
+            if (checkbox.checked) {
+              card.classList.add('selected', 'border-blue-500', 'bg-blue-50');
+            } else {
+              card.classList.remove('selected', 'border-blue-500', 'bg-blue-50');
+            }
+          }
+        });
+      });
+
+      // Checkbox change handler
+      modal.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]').forEach(checkbox => {
+        checkbox.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
+          const card = checkbox.closest('.connector-card');
+          if (card) {
+            if (checkbox.checked) {
+              card.classList.add('selected', 'border-blue-500', 'bg-blue-50');
+            } else {
+              card.classList.remove('selected', 'border-blue-500', 'bg-blue-50');
+            }
+          }
+        });
+      });
+
+      // Individual connector toggle handling
+      modal.querySelectorAll('.edit-connector-toggle').forEach(toggle => {
+        toggle.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
+          e.stopPropagation();
+          const isCurrentlyEnabled = toggle.getAttribute('aria-checked') === 'true';
+          updateToggleState(toggle, !isCurrentlyEnabled);
+        });
+      });
+
+      // Master toggle handling
+      const masterToggle = document.getElementById('editConnectorsToggle');
+      if (masterToggle) {
+        masterToggle.addEventListener('click', () => {
+          const isCurrentlyEnabled = masterToggle.getAttribute('aria-checked') === 'true';
+          const newState = !isCurrentlyEnabled;
+          
+          // Update master toggle
+          updateToggleState(masterToggle, newState);
+          
+          // Update all checked connector toggles
+          modal.querySelectorAll('.connector-card').forEach(card => {
+            const checkbox = card.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"]');
+            const toggle = card.querySelector('.edit-connector-toggle');
+            
+            if (checkbox && checkbox.checked && toggle) {
+              updateToggleState(toggle, newState);
+            }
+          });
+        });
+      }
+    }
+
+    // ==================== NEW CONNECTION MODAL ====================
+
+    // Open New Connection Modal
+    function openNewConnectionModal() {
+      const modal = document.getElementById('newConnectionModal');
+      if (!modal) return;
+
+      // Reset all checkboxes and toggles first
+      resetNewConnectionModal();
+
+      // Show the modal
+      modal.classList.remove('hidden');
+      modal.classList.add('flex');
+    }
+
+    // Reset the New Connection Modal to default state
+    function resetNewConnectionModal() {
+      const modal = document.getElementById('newConnectionModal');
+      if (!modal) return;
+
+      // Reset all checkboxes
+      modal.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]').forEach(cb => {
+        cb.checked = false;
+      });
+
+      // Reset all connector cards
+      modal.querySelectorAll('.connector-card').forEach(card => {
+        card.classList.remove('selected', 'border-blue-500', 'bg-blue-50');
+      });
+
+      // Reset all toggles
+      modal.querySelectorAll('.new-connector-toggle').forEach(toggle => {
+        updateToggleState(toggle, false);
+      });
+
+      // Reset master toggle
+      const masterToggle = document.getElementById('newConnectorsToggle');
+      if (masterToggle) {
+        updateToggleState(masterToggle, false);
+      }
+    }
+
+    // Close New Connection Modal
+    function closeNewConnectionModal() {
+      const modal = document.getElementById('newConnectionModal');
+      if (modal) {
+        modal.classList.add('hidden');
+        modal.classList.remove('flex');
+      }
+    }
+
+    // Connect (Save) New Connections
+    function connectNewConnections() {
+      const modal = document.getElementById('newConnectionModal');
+      if (!modal) return;
+
+      try {
+        // Get advertiser data
+        let advertiser = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('adv_selected_data') || '{}');
+        
+        if (!advertiser.id) {
+          if (window.toast && typeof window.toast.error === 'function') {
+            window.toast.error('Advertiser data not found');
+          }
+          return;
+        }
+
+        // Initialize connectors if not exists
+        if (!advertiser.connectors) {
+          advertiser.connectors = { dsp: [], adServer: [], status: {} };
+        }
+        if (!advertiser.connectors.dsp) advertiser.connectors.dsp = [];
+        if (!advertiser.connectors.adServer) advertiser.connectors.adServer = [];
+        if (!advertiser.connectors.status) advertiser.connectors.status = {};
+
+        // Collect selected platforms and their status from the modal
+        let newConnectionsAdded = 0;
+
+        modal.querySelectorAll('.connector-card').forEach(card => {
+          const checkbox = card.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"]');
+          const toggle = card.querySelector('.new-connector-toggle');
+          
+          if (checkbox && checkbox.checked) {
+            const connectorType = checkbox.name; // 'new-dsp' or 'new-adserver'
+            const connectorValue = checkbox.value;
+            const isConnected = toggle && toggle.getAttribute('aria-checked') === 'true';
+            
+            // Add to appropriate array if not already present
+            if (connectorType === 'new-dsp') {
+              if (!advertiser.connectors.dsp.includes(connectorValue)) {
+                advertiser.connectors.dsp.push(connectorValue);
+                newConnectionsAdded++;
+              }
+            } else if (connectorType === 'new-adserver') {
+              if (!advertiser.connectors.adServer.includes(connectorValue)) {
+                advertiser.connectors.adServer.push(connectorValue);
+                newConnectionsAdded++;
+              }
+            }
+            
+            // Update connection status
+            advertiser.connectors.status[connectorValue] = isConnected ? 'Connected' : 'Disconnected';
+          }
+        });
+
+        if (newConnectionsAdded === 0) {
+          if (window.toast && typeof window.toast.info === 'function') {
+            window.toast.info('No new connections selected');
+          }
+          return;
+        }
+
+        // Save back to localStorage
+        localStorage.setItem('adv_selected_data', JSON.stringify(advertiser));
+
+        // Rebuild the connections table from the updated connectors
+        if (app) {
+          app.adgroups = app.buildPlatformsFromConnectors(advertiser);
+          app.saveAdGroups();
+          app.applyFiltersAndRender();
+        }
+
+        // Show success message
+        if (window.toast && typeof window.toast.success === 'function') {
+          window.toast.success(`${newConnectionsAdded} connection(s) added successfully`);
+        }
+
+        // Close the modal
+        closeNewConnectionModal();
+
+      } catch (error) {
+        console.error('Error adding connections:', error);
+        if (window.toast && typeof window.toast.error === 'function') {
+          window.toast.error('Failed to add connections');
+        }
+      }
+    }
+
+    // Initialize New Connection Modal event listeners
+    function initNewConnectionModal() {
+      const modal = document.getElementById('newConnectionModal');
+      if (!modal) return;
+
+      // Close button
+      const closeBtn = document.getElementById('closeNewConnectionModal');

+        closeBtn.addEventListener('click', closeNewConnectionModal);
+      }
+

+      const cancelBtn = document.getElementById('cancelNewConnection');
+      if (cancelBtn) {
+        cancelBtn.addEventListener('click', closeNewConnectionModal);
+      }
+
+      // Connect button
+      const connectBtn = document.getElementById('connectNewConnection');
+      if (connectBtn) {
+        connectBtn.addEventListener('click', connectNewConnections);
+      }
+
+      // Close on backdrop click
+      modal.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
+        if (e.target === modal) {
+          closeNewConnectionModal();
+        }
+      });
+
+      // Connector card click handling (toggle checkbox)
+      modal.querySelectorAll('.connector-card').forEach(card => {
+        card.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
+          // Don't toggle if clicking on the checkbox, toggle button, or their children
+          if (e.target.closest('input[type="checkbox"]') || e.target.closest('.new-connector-toggle')) {
+            return;
+          }
+          
+          const checkbox = card.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"]');
+          if (checkbox) {
+            checkbox.checked = !checkbox.checked;
+            
+            // Update card styling
+            if (checkbox.checked) {
+              card.classList.add('selected', 'border-blue-500', 'bg-blue-50');
+            } else {
+              card.classList.remove('selected', 'border-blue-500', 'bg-blue-50');
+            }
+          }
+        });
+      });
+
+      // Checkbox change handler
+      modal.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]').forEach(checkbox => {
+        checkbox.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
+          const card = checkbox.closest('.connector-card');
+          if (card) {
+            if (checkbox.checked) {
+              card.classList.add('selected', 'border-blue-500', 'bg-blue-50');
+            } else {
+              card.classList.remove('selected', 'border-blue-500', 'bg-blue-50');
+            }
+          }
+        });
+      });
+
+      // Individual connector toggle handling
+      modal.querySelectorAll('.new-connector-toggle').forEach(toggle => {
+        toggle.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
+          e.stopPropagation();
+          const isCurrentlyEnabled = toggle.getAttribute('aria-checked') === 'true';
+          updateToggleState(toggle, !isCurrentlyEnabled);
+        });
+      });
+
+      // Master toggle handling
+      const masterToggle = document.getElementById('newConnectorsToggle');
+      if (masterToggle) {
+        masterToggle.addEventListener('click', () => {
+          const isCurrentlyEnabled = masterToggle.getAttribute('aria-checked') === 'true';
+          const newState = !isCurrentlyEnabled;
+          
+          // Update master toggle
+          updateToggleState(masterToggle, newState);
+          
+          // Update all checked connector toggles
+          modal.querySelectorAll('.connector-card').forEach(card => {
+            const checkbox = card.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"]');
+            const toggle = card.querySelector('.new-connector-toggle');
+            
+            if (checkbox && checkbox.checked && toggle) {
+              updateToggleState(toggle, newState);
+            }
+          });
+        });
+      }
+
+      // Wire up the "New Connection" button in the toolbar
+      const createBtn = document.getElementById('createBtn');

+        createBtn.addEventListener('click', openNewConnectionModal);
+      }
+    }

+    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
+      initEditConnectionsModal();
+      initNewConnectionModal();
+    });
